     429            8 : /** @internal */
     430            8 : export function isBuildInfoFile(file: string) {
     431            8 :     return fileExtensionIs(file, Extension.TsBuildInfo);
     432            8 : }
     433            8 : 
     434            8 : /**
     435            8 :  * Iterates over the source files that are expected to have an emit output.
     436            8 :  *
     437            8 :  * @param host An EmitHost.
     438            8 :  * @param action The action to execute.
     439            8 :  * @param sourceFilesOrTargetSourceFile
     440            8 :  *   If an array, the full list of source files to emit.
     441            8 :  *   Else, calls `getSourceFilesToEmit` with the (optional) target source file to determine the list of source files to emit.
     442            8 :  *
     443            8 :  * @internal
     444            8 :  */
     445            8 : export function forEachEmittedFile<T>(
     446            8 :     host: EmitHost,
     447            8 :     action: (emitFileNames: EmitFileNames, sourceFileOrBundle: SourceFile | Bundle | undefined) => T,
     448            8 :     sourceFilesOrTargetSourceFile?: readonly SourceFile[] | SourceFile,
     449            8 :     forceDtsEmit = false,
     450            8 :     onlyBuildInfo?: boolean,
     451            8 :     includeBuildInfo?: boolean,
     452            8 : ) {
     453            8 :     const sourceFiles = isArray(sourceFilesOrTargetSourceFile) ? sourceFilesOrTargetSourceFile : getSourceFilesToEmit(host, sourceFilesOrTargetSourceFile, forceDtsEmit);
     454            8 :     const options = host.getCompilerOptions();
     455            8 :     if (!onlyBuildInfo) {
     456            8 :         if (options.outFile) {
     457            8 :             if (sourceFiles.length) {
     458            8 :                 const bundle = factory.createBundle(sourceFiles);
     459            8 :                 const result = action(getOutputPathsFor(bundle, host, forceDtsEmit), bundle);
     460            8 :                 if (result) {
     461            8 :                     return result;
     462            8 :                 }
     463            8 :             }
     464            8 :         }
     465            8 :         else {
     466            8 :             for (const sourceFile of sourceFiles) {
     467            8 :                 const result = action(getOutputPathsFor(sourceFile, host, forceDtsEmit), sourceFile);
     468            8 :                 if (result) {
     469            8 :                     return result;
     470            8 :                 }
     471            8 :             }
     472            8 :         }
     473            8 :     }
     474            8 :     if (includeBuildInfo) {
     475            8 :         const buildInfoPath = getTsBuildInfoEmitOutputFilePath(options);
     476            8 :         if (buildInfoPath) return action({ buildInfoPath }, /*sourceFileOrBundle*/ undefined);
     477            8 :     }
     478            8 : }
     479            8 : 
     480            8 : export function getTsBuildInfoEmitOutputFilePath(options: CompilerOptions) {
     481            8 :     const configFile = options.configFilePath;
     482            8 :     if (!isIncrementalCompilation(options)) return undefined;
     483            8 :     if (options.tsBuildInfoFile) return options.tsBuildInfoFile;
     484            8 :     const outPath = options.outFile;
     485            8 :     let buildInfoExtensionLess: string;
     486            8 :     if (outPath) {
     487            8 :         buildInfoExtensionLess = removeFileExtension(outPath);
     488            8 :     }
     489            8 :     else {
     490            8 :         if (!configFile) return undefined;
     491            8 :         const configFileExtensionLess = removeFileExtension(configFile);
     492            8 :         buildInfoExtensionLess = options.outDir ?
     493            8 :             options.rootDir ?
     494            8 :                 resolvePath(options.outDir, getRelativePathFromDirectory(options.rootDir, configFileExtensionLess, /*ignoreCase*/ true)) :
     495            8 :                 combinePaths(options.outDir, getBaseFileName(configFileExtensionLess)) :
     496            8 :             configFileExtensionLess;
     497            8 :     }
     498            8 :     return buildInfoExtensionLess + Extension.TsBuildInfo;
     499            8 : }
     500            8 : 
     501            8 : /** @internal */
     502            8 : export function getOutputPathsForBundle(options: CompilerOptions, forceDtsPaths: boolean): EmitFileNames {
     503            8 :     const outPath = options.outFile!;
     504            8 :     const jsFilePath = options.emitDeclarationOnly ? undefined : outPath;
     505            8 :     const sourceMapFilePath = jsFilePath && getSourceMapFilePath(jsFilePath, options);
     506            8 :     const declarationFilePath = (forceDtsPaths || getEmitDeclarations(options)) ? removeFileExtension(outPath) + Extension.Dts : undefined;
     507            8 :     const declarationMapPath = declarationFilePath && getAreDeclarationMapsEnabled(options) ? declarationFilePath + ".map" : undefined;
     508            8 :     return { jsFilePath, sourceMapFilePath, declarationFilePath, declarationMapPath };
     509            8 : }
     510            8 : 
     511            8 : /** @internal */
     512            8 : export function getOutputPathsFor(sourceFile: SourceFile | Bundle, host: EmitHost, forceDtsPaths: boolean): EmitFileNames {
     513            8 :     const options = host.getCompilerOptions();
     514            8 :     if (sourceFile.kind === SyntaxKind.Bundle) {
     515            8 :         return getOutputPathsForBundle(options, forceDtsPaths);
     516            8 :     }
     517            8 :     else {
     518            8 :         const ownOutputFilePath = getOwnEmitOutputFilePath(sourceFile.fileName, host, getOutputExtension(sourceFile.fileName, options));
     519            8 :         const isJsonFile = isJsonSourceFile(sourceFile);
     520            8 :         // If json file emits to the same location skip writing it, if emitDeclarationOnly skip writing it
     521            8 :         const isJsonEmittedToSameLocation = isJsonFile &&
     522            8 :             comparePaths(sourceFile.fileName, ownOutputFilePath, host.getCurrentDirectory(), !host.useCaseSensitiveFileNames()) === Comparison.EqualTo;
     523            8 :         const jsFilePath = options.emitDeclarationOnly || isJsonEmittedToSameLocation ? undefined : ownOutputFilePath;
     524            8 :         const sourceMapFilePath = !jsFilePath || isJsonSourceFile(sourceFile) ? undefined : getSourceMapFilePath(jsFilePath, options);
     525            8 :         const declarationFilePath = (forceDtsPaths || (getEmitDeclarations(options) && !isJsonFile)) ? getDeclarationEmitOutputFilePath(sourceFile.fileName, host) : undefined;
     526            8 :         const declarationMapPath = declarationFilePath && getAreDeclarationMapsEnabled(options) ? declarationFilePath + ".map" : undefined;
     527            8 :         return { jsFilePath, sourceMapFilePath, declarationFilePath, declarationMapPath };
     528            8 :     }
     529            8 : }
     530            8 : 
     531            8 : function getSourceMapFilePath(jsFilePath: string, options: CompilerOptions) {
     532            8 :     return (options.sourceMap && !options.inlineSourceMap) ? jsFilePath + ".map" : undefined;
     533            8 : }
     534            8 : 
     535            8 : /** @internal */
     536            8 : export function getOutputExtension(fileName: string, options: Pick<CompilerOptions, "jsx">): Extension {
     537            8 :     return fileExtensionIs(fileName, Extension.Json) ? Extension.Json :
     538            8 :         options.jsx === JsxEmit.Preserve && fileExtensionIsOneOf(fileName, [Extension.Jsx, Extension.Tsx]) ? Extension.Jsx :
     539            8 :         fileExtensionIsOneOf(fileName, [Extension.Mts, Extension.Mjs]) ? Extension.Mjs :
     540            8 :         fileExtensionIsOneOf(fileName, [Extension.Cts, Extension.Cjs]) ? Extension.Cjs :
     541            8 :         Extension.Js;
     542            8 : }
     543            8 : 
     544            8 : function getOutputPathWithoutChangingExt(
     545            8 :     inputFileName: string,
     546            8 :     ignoreCase: boolean,
     547            8 :     outputDir: string | undefined,
     548            8 :     getCommonSourceDirectory: () => string,
     549            8 : ): string {
     550            8 :     return outputDir ?
     551            8 :         resolvePath(
     552            8 :             outputDir,
     553            8 :             getRelativePathFromDirectory(getCommonSourceDirectory(), inputFileName, ignoreCase),
     554            8 :         ) :
     555            8 :         inputFileName;
     556            8 : }
     557            8 : 
     558            8 : /** @internal */
     559            8 : export function getOutputDeclarationFileName(inputFileName: string, configFile: ParsedCommandLine, ignoreCase: boolean, getCommonSourceDirectory = () => getCommonSourceDirectoryOfConfig(configFile, ignoreCase)) {
     560            8 :     return getOutputDeclarationFileNameWorker(inputFileName, configFile.options, ignoreCase, getCommonSourceDirectory);
     561            8 : }
     562            8 : 
     563            8 : /** @internal */
     564            8 : export function getOutputDeclarationFileNameWorker(inputFileName: string, options: CompilerOptions, ignoreCase: boolean, getCommonSourceDirectory: () => string) {
     565            8 :     return changeExtension(
     566            8 :         getOutputPathWithoutChangingExt(inputFileName, ignoreCase, options.declarationDir || options.outDir, getCommonSourceDirectory),
     567            8 :         getDeclarationEmitExtensionForPath(inputFileName),
     568            8 :     );
     569            8 : }
     570            8 : 
     571            8 : function getOutputJSFileName(inputFileName: string, configFile: ParsedCommandLine, ignoreCase: boolean, getCommonSourceDirectory = () => getCommonSourceDirectoryOfConfig(configFile, ignoreCase)) {
     572            8 :     if (configFile.options.emitDeclarationOnly) return undefined;
     573            8 :     const isJsonFile = fileExtensionIs(inputFileName, Extension.Json);
     574            8 :     const outputFileName = getOutputJSFileNameWorker(inputFileName, configFile.options, ignoreCase, getCommonSourceDirectory);
     575            8 :     return !isJsonFile || comparePaths(inputFileName, outputFileName, Debug.checkDefined(configFile.options.configFilePath), ignoreCase) !== Comparison.EqualTo ?
     576            8 :         outputFileName :
     577            8 :         undefined;
     578            8 : }

     609            8 : function getOwnOutputFileNames(configFile: ParsedCommandLine, inputFileName: string, ignoreCase: boolean, addOutput: ReturnType<typeof createAddOutput>["addOutput"], getCommonSourceDirectory?: () => string) {
     610            8 :     if (isDeclarationFileName(inputFileName)) return;

     613            8 :     if (fileExtensionIs(inputFileName, Extension.Json)) return;

     616            8 :     }

     626            8 : /** @internal */
     627            8 : export function getCommonSourceDirectory(
     628            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
     629            8 :     emittedFiles: () => readonly string[],
     630            8 :     currentDirectory: string,
     631            8 :     getCanonicalFileName: GetCanonicalFileName,
     632            8 :     checkSourceFilesBelongToPath?: (commonSourceDirectory: string) => void,
     633            8 : ): string {
     634            8 :     let commonSourceDirectory;
     635            8 :     if (options.rootDir) {
     636            8 :         // If a rootDir is specified use it as the commonSourceDirectory
     637            8 :         commonSourceDirectory = getNormalizedAbsolutePath(options.rootDir, currentDirectory);
     638            8 :         checkSourceFilesBelongToPath?.(options.rootDir);
     639            8 :     }
     640            8 :     else if (options.composite && options.configFilePath) {
     641            8 :         // Project compilations never infer their root from the input source paths
     642            8 :         commonSourceDirectory = getDirectoryPath(normalizeSlashes(options.configFilePath));
     643            8 :         checkSourceFilesBelongToPath?.(commonSourceDirectory);
     644            8 :     }
     645            8 :     else {
     646            8 :         commonSourceDirectory = computeCommonSourceDirectoryOfFilenames(emittedFiles(), currentDirectory, getCanonicalFileName);
     647            8 :     }
     648            8 : 
     649            8 :     if (commonSourceDirectory && commonSourceDirectory[commonSourceDirectory.length - 1] !== directorySeparator) {
     650            8 :         // Make sure directory path ends with directory separator so this string can directly
     651            8 :         // used to replace with "" to get the relative path of the source file and the relative path doesn't
     652            8 :         // start with / making it rooted path
     653            8 :         commonSourceDirectory += directorySeparator;
     654            8 :     }
     655            8 :     return commonSourceDirectory;
     656            8 : }

     658            8 : /** @internal */

     661            8 :         options,
     662            8 :         () => filter(fileNames, file => !(options.noEmitForJsFiles && fileExtensionIsOneOf(file, supportedJSExtensionsFlat)) && !isDeclarationFileName(file)),
     663            8 :         getDirectoryPath(normalizeSlashes(Debug.checkDefined(options.configFilePath))),
     664            8 :         createGetCanonicalFileName(!ignoreCase),
     665            8 :     );
     666            8 : }

     697            8 : /** @internal */
     698            8 : export function getFirstProjectOutput(configFile: ParsedCommandLine, ignoreCase: boolean): string {
     699            8 :     if (configFile.options.outFile) {
     700            8 :         const { jsFilePath, declarationFilePath } = getOutputPathsForBundle(configFile.options, /*forceDtsPaths*/ false);
     701            8 :         return Debug.checkDefined(jsFilePath || declarationFilePath, `project ${configFile.options.configFilePath} expected to have at least one output`);
     702            8 :     }
     703            8 : 
     704            8 :     const getCommonSourceDirectory = memoize(() => getCommonSourceDirectoryOfConfig(configFile, ignoreCase));
     705            8 :     for (const inputFileName of configFile.fileNames) {
     706            8 :         if (isDeclarationFileName(inputFileName)) continue;
     707            8 :         const jsFilePath = getOutputJSFileName(inputFileName, configFile, ignoreCase, getCommonSourceDirectory);
     708            8 :         if (jsFilePath) return jsFilePath;
     709            8 :         if (fileExtensionIs(inputFileName, Extension.Json)) continue;
     710            8 :         if (getEmitDeclarations(configFile.options)) {
     711            8 :             return getOutputDeclarationFileName(inputFileName, configFile, ignoreCase, getCommonSourceDirectory);
     712            8 :         }
     713            8 :     }
     714            8 :     const buildInfoPath = getTsBuildInfoEmitOutputFilePath(configFile.options);
     715            8 :     if (buildInfoPath) return buildInfoPath;
     716            8 :     return Debug.fail(`project ${configFile.options.configFilePath} expected to have at least one output`);
     717            8 : }

     724            8 : /** @internal */
     725            8 : // targetSourceFile is when users only want one file in entire project to be emitted. This is used in compileOnSave feature
     726            8 : export function emitFiles(
     727            8 :     resolver: EmitResolver,
     728            8 :     host: EmitHost,
     729            8 :     targetSourceFile: SourceFile | undefined,
     730            8 :     { scriptTransformers, declarationTransformers }: EmitTransformers,
     731            8 :     emitOnly: boolean | EmitOnly | undefined,
     732            8 :     onlyBuildInfo: boolean,
     733            8 :     forceDtsEmit?: boolean,
     734            8 :     skipBuildInfo?: boolean,
     735            8 : ): EmitResult {
     736            8 :     // Why var? It avoids TDZ checks in the runtime which can be costly.
     737            8 :     // See: https://github.com/microsoft/TypeScript/issues/52924
     738            8 :     /* eslint-disable no-var */
     739            8 :     var compilerOptions = host.getCompilerOptions();
     740            8 :     var sourceMapDataList: SourceMapEmitResult[] | undefined = (compilerOptions.sourceMap || compilerOptions.inlineSourceMap || getAreDeclarationMapsEnabled(compilerOptions)) ? [] : undefined;
     741            8 :     var emittedFilesList: string[] | undefined = compilerOptions.listEmittedFiles ? [] : undefined;
     742            8 :     var emitterDiagnostics = createDiagnosticCollection();
     743            8 :     var newLine = getNewLineCharacter(compilerOptions);
     744            8 :     var writer = createTextWriter(newLine);
     745            8 :     var { enter, exit } = performance.createTimer("printTime", "beforePrint", "afterPrint");
     746            8 :     var emitSkipped = false;
     747            8 :     /* eslint-enable no-var */
     748            8 : 
     749            8 :     // Emit each output file
     750            8 :     enter();
     751            8 :     forEachEmittedFile(
     752            8 :         host,
     753            8 :         emitSourceFileOrBundle,
     754            8 :         getSourceFilesToEmit(host, targetSourceFile, forceDtsEmit),
     755            8 :         forceDtsEmit,
     756            8 :         onlyBuildInfo,
     757            8 :         !targetSourceFile && !skipBuildInfo,
     758            8 :     );
     759            8 :     exit();
     760            8 : 
     761            8 :     return {
     762            8 :         emitSkipped,
     763            8 :         diagnostics: emitterDiagnostics.getDiagnostics(),
     764            8 :         emittedFiles: emittedFilesList,
     765            8 :         sourceMaps: sourceMapDataList,
     766            8 :     };
     767            8 : 
     768            8 :     function emitSourceFileOrBundle({ jsFilePath, sourceMapFilePath, declarationFilePath, declarationMapPath, buildInfoPath }: EmitFileNames, sourceFileOrBundle: SourceFile | Bundle | undefined) {
     769            8 :         tracing?.push(tracing.Phase.Emit, "emitJsFileOrBundle", { jsFilePath });
     770            8 :         emitJsFileOrBundle(sourceFileOrBundle, jsFilePath, sourceMapFilePath);
     771            8 :         tracing?.pop();
     772            8 : 
     773            8 :         tracing?.push(tracing.Phase.Emit, "emitDeclarationFileOrBundle", { declarationFilePath });
     774            8 :         emitDeclarationFileOrBundle(sourceFileOrBundle, declarationFilePath, declarationMapPath);
     775            8 :         tracing?.pop();
     776            8 : 
     777            8 :         tracing?.push(tracing.Phase.Emit, "emitBuildInfo", { buildInfoPath });
     778            8 :         emitBuildInfo(buildInfoPath);
     779            8 :         tracing?.pop();
     780            8 :     }
     781            8 : 
     782            8 :     function emitBuildInfo(buildInfoPath: string | undefined) {
     783            8 :         // Write build information if applicable
     784            8 :         if (!buildInfoPath || targetSourceFile) return;
     785            8 :         if (host.isEmitBlocked(buildInfoPath)) {
     786            8 :             emitSkipped = true;
     787            8 :             return;
     788            8 :         }
     789            8 :         const buildInfo = host.getBuildInfo() || { version };
     790            8 :         // Pass buildinfo as additional data to avoid having to reparse
     791            8 :         writeFile(host, emitterDiagnostics, buildInfoPath, getBuildInfoText(buildInfo), /*writeByteOrderMark*/ false, /*sourceFiles*/ undefined, { buildInfo });
     792            8 :         emittedFilesList?.push(buildInfoPath);
     793            8 :     }
     794            8 : 
     795            8 :     function emitJsFileOrBundle(
     796            8 :         sourceFileOrBundle: SourceFile | Bundle | undefined,
     797            8 :         jsFilePath: string | undefined,
     798            8 :         sourceMapFilePath: string | undefined,
     799            8 :     ) {
     800            8 :         if (!sourceFileOrBundle || emitOnly || !jsFilePath) {
     801            8 :             return;
     802            8 :         }
     803            8 : 
     804            8 :         // Make sure not to write js file and source map file if any of them cannot be written
     805            8 :         if (host.isEmitBlocked(jsFilePath) || compilerOptions.noEmit) {
     806            8 :             emitSkipped = true;
     807            8 :             return;
     808            8 :         }
     809            8 : 
     810            8 :         (isSourceFile(sourceFileOrBundle) ? [sourceFileOrBundle] : filter(sourceFileOrBundle.sourceFiles, isSourceFileNotJson)).forEach(
     811            8 :             sourceFile => {
     812            8 :                 if (
     813            8 :                     compilerOptions.noCheck ||
     814            8 :                     !canIncludeBindAndCheckDiagnsotics(sourceFile, compilerOptions)
     815            8 :                 ) markLinkedReferences(sourceFile);
     816            8 :             },
     817            8 :         );
     818            8 : 
     819            8 :         // Transform the source files
     820            8 :         const transform = transformNodes(resolver, host, factory, compilerOptions, [sourceFileOrBundle], scriptTransformers, /*allowDtsFiles*/ false);
     821            8 : 
     822            8 :         const printerOptions: PrinterOptions = {
     823            8 :             removeComments: compilerOptions.removeComments,
     824            8 :             newLine: compilerOptions.newLine,
     825            8 :             noEmitHelpers: compilerOptions.noEmitHelpers,
     826            8 :             module: getEmitModuleKind(compilerOptions),
     827            8 :             moduleResolution: getEmitModuleResolutionKind(compilerOptions),
     828            8 :             target: getEmitScriptTarget(compilerOptions),
     829            8 :             sourceMap: compilerOptions.sourceMap,
     830            8 :             inlineSourceMap: compilerOptions.inlineSourceMap,
     831            8 :             inlineSources: compilerOptions.inlineSources,
     832            8 :             extendedDiagnostics: compilerOptions.extendedDiagnostics,
     833            8 :         };
     834            8 : 
     835            8 :         // Create a printer to print the nodes
     836            8 :         const printer = createPrinter(printerOptions, {
     837            8 :             // resolver hooks
     838            8 :             hasGlobalName: resolver.hasGlobalName,
     839            8 : 
     840            8 :             // transform hooks
     841            8 :             onEmitNode: transform.emitNodeWithNotification,
     842            8 :             isEmitNotificationEnabled: transform.isEmitNotificationEnabled,
     843            8 :             substituteNode: transform.substituteNode,
     844            8 :         });
     845            8 : 
     846            8 :         Debug.assert(transform.transformed.length === 1, "Should only see one output from the transform");
     847            8 :         printSourceFileOrBundle(jsFilePath, sourceMapFilePath, transform, printer, compilerOptions);
     848            8 : 
     849            8 :         // Clean up emit nodes on parse tree
     850            8 :         transform.dispose();
     851            8 : 
     852            8 :         if (emittedFilesList) {
     853            8 :             emittedFilesList.push(jsFilePath);
     854            8 :             if (sourceMapFilePath) {
     855            8 :                 emittedFilesList.push(sourceMapFilePath);
     856            8 :             }
     857            8 :         }
     858            8 :     }
     859            8 : 
     860            8 :     function emitDeclarationFileOrBundle(
     861            8 :         sourceFileOrBundle: SourceFile | Bundle | undefined,
     862            8 :         declarationFilePath: string | undefined,
     863            8 :         declarationMapPath: string | undefined,
     864            8 :     ) {
     865            8 :         if (!sourceFileOrBundle || emitOnly === EmitOnly.Js) return;
     866            8 :         if (!declarationFilePath) {
     867            8 :             if (emitOnly || compilerOptions.emitDeclarationOnly) emitSkipped = true;
     868            8 :             return;
     869            8 :         }
     870            8 :         const sourceFiles = isSourceFile(sourceFileOrBundle) ? [sourceFileOrBundle] : sourceFileOrBundle.sourceFiles;
     871            8 :         const filesForEmit = forceDtsEmit ? sourceFiles : filter(sourceFiles, isSourceFileNotJson);
     872            8 :         // Setup and perform the transformation to retrieve declarations from the input files
     873            8 :         const inputListOrBundle = compilerOptions.outFile ? [factory.createBundle(filesForEmit)] : filesForEmit;
     874            8 :         // Checker wont collect the linked aliases since thats only done when declaration is enabled and checking is performed.
     875            8 :         // Do that here when emitting only dts files
     876            8 :         filesForEmit.forEach(sourceFile => {
     877            8 :             if (
     878            8 :                 (emitOnly && !getEmitDeclarations(compilerOptions)) ||
     879            8 :                 compilerOptions.noCheck ||
     880            8 :                 emitResolverSkipsTypeChecking(emitOnly, forceDtsEmit) ||
     881            8 :                 !canIncludeBindAndCheckDiagnsotics(sourceFile, compilerOptions)
     882            8 :             ) {
     883            8 :                 collectLinkedAliases(sourceFile);
     884            8 :             }
     885            8 :         });
     886            8 : 
     887            8 :         const declarationTransform = transformNodes(resolver, host, factory, compilerOptions, inputListOrBundle, declarationTransformers, /*allowDtsFiles*/ false);
     888            8 :         if (length(declarationTransform.diagnostics)) {
     889            8 :             for (const diagnostic of declarationTransform.diagnostics!) {
     890            8 :                 emitterDiagnostics.add(diagnostic);
     891            8 :             }
     892            8 :         }
     893            8 : 
     894            8 :         const declBlocked = (!!declarationTransform.diagnostics && !!declarationTransform.diagnostics.length) || !!host.isEmitBlocked(declarationFilePath) || !!compilerOptions.noEmit;
     895            8 :         emitSkipped = emitSkipped || declBlocked;
     896            8 :         if (!declBlocked || forceDtsEmit) {
     897            8 :             Debug.assert(declarationTransform.transformed.length === 1, "Should only see one output from the decl transform");
     898            8 :             const printerOptions: PrinterOptions = {
     899            8 :                 removeComments: compilerOptions.removeComments,
     900            8 :                 newLine: compilerOptions.newLine,
     901            8 :                 noEmitHelpers: true,
     902            8 :                 module: compilerOptions.module,
     903            8 :                 moduleResolution: compilerOptions.moduleResolution,
     904            8 :                 target: compilerOptions.target,
     905            8 :                 sourceMap: !forceDtsEmit && compilerOptions.declarationMap,
     906            8 :                 inlineSourceMap: compilerOptions.inlineSourceMap,
     907            8 :                 extendedDiagnostics: compilerOptions.extendedDiagnostics,
     908            8 :                 onlyPrintJsDocStyle: true,
     909            8 :                 omitBraceSourceMapPositions: true,
     910            8 :             };
     911            8 : 
     912            8 :             const declarationPrinter = createPrinter(printerOptions, {
     913            8 :                 // resolver hooks
     914            8 :                 hasGlobalName: resolver.hasGlobalName,
     915            8 : 
     916            8 :                 // transform hooks
     917            8 :                 onEmitNode: declarationTransform.emitNodeWithNotification,
     918            8 :                 isEmitNotificationEnabled: declarationTransform.isEmitNotificationEnabled,
     919            8 :                 substituteNode: declarationTransform.substituteNode,
     920            8 :             });
     921            8 :             printSourceFileOrBundle(
     922            8 :                 declarationFilePath,
     923            8 :                 declarationMapPath,
     924            8 :                 declarationTransform,
     925            8 :                 declarationPrinter,
     926            8 :                 {
     927            8 :                     sourceMap: printerOptions.sourceMap,
     928            8 :                     sourceRoot: compilerOptions.sourceRoot,
     929            8 :                     mapRoot: compilerOptions.mapRoot,
     930            8 :                     extendedDiagnostics: compilerOptions.extendedDiagnostics,
     931            8 :                     // Explicitly do not passthru either `inline` option
     932            8 :                 },
     933            8 :             );
     934            8 :             if (emittedFilesList) {
     935            8 :                 emittedFilesList.push(declarationFilePath);
     936            8 :                 if (declarationMapPath) {
     937            8 :                     emittedFilesList.push(declarationMapPath);
     938            8 :                 }
     939            8 :             }
     940            8 :         }
     941            8 :         declarationTransform.dispose();
     942            8 :     }
     943            8 : 
     944            8 :     function collectLinkedAliases(node: Node) {
     945            8 :         if (isExportAssignment(node)) {
     946            8 :             if (node.expression.kind === SyntaxKind.Identifier) {
     947            8 :                 resolver.collectLinkedAliases(node.expression as Identifier, /*setVisibility*/ true);
     948            8 :             }
     949            8 :             return;
     950            8 :         }
     951            8 :         else if (isExportSpecifier(node)) {
     952            8 :             resolver.collectLinkedAliases(node.propertyName || node.name, /*setVisibility*/ true);
     953            8 :             return;
     954            8 :         }
     955            8 :         forEachChild(node, collectLinkedAliases);
     956            8 :     }
     957            8 : 
     958            8 :     function markLinkedReferences(file: SourceFile) {
     959            8 :         ts.forEachChildRecursively(file, n => {
     960            8 :             if (isImportEqualsDeclaration(n) && !(ts.getSyntacticModifierFlags(n) & ts.ModifierFlags.Export)) return "skip"; // These are deferred and marked in a chain when referenced
     961            8 :             if (ts.isImportDeclaration(n)) return "skip"; // likewise, these are ultimately what get marked by calls on other nodes - we want to skip them
     962            8 :             resolver.markLinkedReferences(n);
     963            8 :         });
     964            8 :     }
     965            8 : 
     966            8 :     function printSourceFileOrBundle(jsFilePath: string, sourceMapFilePath: string | undefined, transform: TransformationResult<SourceFile | Bundle>, printer: Printer, mapOptions: SourceMapOptions) {
     967            8 :         const sourceFileOrBundle = transform.transformed[0];
     968            8 :         const bundle = sourceFileOrBundle.kind === SyntaxKind.Bundle ? sourceFileOrBundle : undefined;
     969            8 :         const sourceFile = sourceFileOrBundle.kind === SyntaxKind.SourceFile ? sourceFileOrBundle : undefined;
     970            8 :         const sourceFiles = bundle ? bundle.sourceFiles : [sourceFile!];
     971            8 : 
     972            8 :         let sourceMapGenerator: SourceMapGenerator | undefined;
     973            8 :         if (shouldEmitSourceMaps(mapOptions, sourceFileOrBundle)) {
     974            8 :             sourceMapGenerator = createSourceMapGenerator(
     975            8 :                 host,
     976            8 :                 getBaseFileName(normalizeSlashes(jsFilePath)),
     977            8 :                 getSourceRoot(mapOptions),
     978            8 :                 getSourceMapDirectory(mapOptions, jsFilePath, sourceFile),
     979            8 :                 mapOptions,
     980            8 :             );
     981            8 :         }
     982            8 : 
     983            8 :         if (bundle) {
     984            8 :             printer.writeBundle(bundle, writer, sourceMapGenerator);
     985            8 :         }
     986            8 :         else {
     987            8 :             printer.writeFile(sourceFile!, writer, sourceMapGenerator);
     988            8 :         }
     989            8 : 
     990            8 :         let sourceMapUrlPos;
     991            8 :         if (sourceMapGenerator) {
     992            8 :             if (sourceMapDataList) {
     993            8 :                 sourceMapDataList.push({
     994            8 :                     inputSourceFileNames: sourceMapGenerator.getSources(),
     995            8 :                     sourceMap: sourceMapGenerator.toJSON(),
     996            8 :                 });
     997            8 :             }
     998            8 : 
     999            8 :             const sourceMappingURL = getSourceMappingURL(
    1000            8 :                 mapOptions,
    1001            8 :                 sourceMapGenerator,
    1002            8 :                 jsFilePath,
    1003            8 :                 sourceMapFilePath,
    1004            8 :                 sourceFile,
    1005            8 :             );
    1006            8 : 
    1007            8 :             if (sourceMappingURL) {
    1008            8 :                 if (!writer.isAtStartOfLine()) writer.rawWrite(newLine);
    1009            8 :                 sourceMapUrlPos = writer.getTextPos();
    1010            8 :                 writer.writeComment(`//# ${"sourceMappingURL"}=${sourceMappingURL}`); // Tools can sometimes see this line as a source mapping url comment
    1011            8 :             }
    1012            8 : 
    1013            8 :             // Write the source map
    1014            8 :             if (sourceMapFilePath) {
    1015            8 :                 const sourceMap = sourceMapGenerator.toString();
    1016            8 :                 writeFile(host, emitterDiagnostics, sourceMapFilePath, sourceMap, /*writeByteOrderMark*/ false, sourceFiles);
    1017            8 :             }
    1018            8 :         }
    1019            8 :         else {
    1020            8 :             writer.writeLine();
    1021            8 :         }
    1022            8 : 
    1023            8 :         // Write the output file
    1024            8 :         const text = writer.getText();
    1025            8 :         writeFile(host, emitterDiagnostics, jsFilePath, text, !!compilerOptions.emitBOM, sourceFiles, { sourceMapUrlPos, diagnostics: transform.diagnostics });
    1026            8 : 
    1027            8 :         // Reset state
    1028            8 :         writer.clear();
    1029            8 :     }
    1030            8 : 
    1031            8 :     interface SourceMapOptions {
    1032            8 :         sourceMap?: boolean;
    1033            8 :         inlineSourceMap?: boolean;
    1034            8 :         inlineSources?: boolean;
    1035            8 :         sourceRoot?: string;
    1036            8 :         mapRoot?: string;
    1037            8 :         extendedDiagnostics?: boolean;
    1038            8 :     }

    1052            8 :     function getSourceMapDirectory(mapOptions: SourceMapOptions, filePath: string, sourceFile: SourceFile | undefined) {
    1053            8 :         if (mapOptions.sourceRoot) return host.getCommonSourceDirectory();
    1054            8 :         if (mapOptions.mapRoot) {
    1055            8 :             let sourceMapDir = normalizeSlashes(mapOptions.mapRoot);
    1056            8 :             if (sourceFile) {
    1057            8 :                 // For modules or multiple emit files the mapRoot will have directory structure like the sources
    1058            8 :                 // So if src\a.ts and src\lib\b.ts are compiled together user would be moving the maps into mapRoot\a.js.map and mapRoot\lib\b.js.map
    1059            8 :                 sourceMapDir = getDirectoryPath(getSourceFilePathInNewDir(sourceFile.fileName, host, sourceMapDir));
    1060            8 :             }
    1061            8 :             if (getRootLength(sourceMapDir) === 0) {
    1062            8 :                 // The relative paths are relative to the common directory
    1063            8 :                 sourceMapDir = combinePaths(host.getCommonSourceDirectory(), sourceMapDir);
    1064            8 :             }
    1065            8 :             return sourceMapDir;
    1066            8 :         }
    1067            8 :         return getDirectoryPath(normalizePath(filePath));
    1068            8 :     }

    1071            8 :         if (mapOptions.inlineSourceMap) {
    1072            8 :             // Encode the sourceMap into the sourceMap url
    1073            8 :             const sourceMapText = sourceMapGenerator.toString();

    1075            8 :             return `data:application/json;base64,${base64SourceMapText}`;
    1076            8 :         }
    1077            8 : 
    1078            8 :         const sourceMapFile = getBaseFileName(normalizeSlashes(Debug.checkDefined(sourceMapFilePath)));
    1079            8 :         if (mapOptions.mapRoot) {
    1080            8 :             let sourceMapDir = normalizeSlashes(mapOptions.mapRoot);
    1081            8 :             if (sourceFile) {
    1082            8 :                 // For modules or multiple emit files the mapRoot will have directory structure like the sources
    1083            8 :                 // So if src\a.ts and src\lib\b.ts are compiled together user would be moving the maps into mapRoot\a.js.map and mapRoot\lib\b.js.map
    1084            8 :                 sourceMapDir = getDirectoryPath(getSourceFilePathInNewDir(sourceFile.fileName, host, sourceMapDir));
    1085            8 :             }
    1086            8 :             if (getRootLength(sourceMapDir) === 0) {
    1087            8 :                 // The relative paths are relative to the common directory
    1088            8 :                 sourceMapDir = combinePaths(host.getCommonSourceDirectory(), sourceMapDir);
    1089            8 :                 return encodeURI(
    1090            8 :                     getRelativePathToDirectoryOrUrl(

    1092            8 :                         combinePaths(sourceMapDir, sourceMapFile), // this is where user expects to see sourceMap

    1095            8 :                         /*isAbsolutePathAnUrl*/ true,
    1096            8 :                     ),

    1098            8 :             }
    1099            8 :             else {
    1100            8 :                 return encodeURI(combinePaths(sourceMapDir, sourceMapFile));
    1101            8 :             }
    1102            8 :         }
    1103            8 :         return encodeURI(sourceMapFile);
    1104            8 :     }

    1267            8 :     function printNode(hint: EmitHint, node: Node, sourceFile: SourceFile): string {

    1464            8 :             !isSourceFile(node) &&

    1466            8 :     }

    1468            8 :     function getPipelinePhase(phase: PipelinePhase, emitHint: EmitHint, node: Node) {
    1469            8 :         switch (phase) {
    1470            8 :             case PipelinePhase.Notification:
    1471            8 :                 if (onEmitNode !== noEmitNotification && (!isEmitNotificationEnabled || isEmitNotificationEnabled(node))) {
    1472            8 :                     return pipelineEmitWithNotification;
    1473            8 :                 }
    1474            8 :                 // falls through
    1475            8 :             case PipelinePhase.Substitution:
    1476            8 :                 if (substituteNode !== noEmitSubstitution && (lastSubstitution = substituteNode(emitHint, node) || node) !== node) {
    1477            8 :                     if (currentParenthesizerRule) {
    1478            8 :                         lastSubstitution = currentParenthesizerRule(lastSubstitution);
    1479            8 :                     }
    1480            8 :                     return pipelineEmitWithSubstitution;
    1481            8 :                 }
    1482            8 :                 // falls through
    1483            8 :             case PipelinePhase.Comments:
    1484            8 :                 if (shouldEmitComments(node)) {
    1485            8 :                     return pipelineEmitWithComments;
    1486            8 :                 }
    1487            8 :                 // falls through
    1488            8 :             case PipelinePhase.SourceMaps:
    1489            8 :                 if (shouldEmitSourceMaps(node)) {
    1490            8 :                     return pipelineEmitWithSourceMaps;
    1491            8 :                 }
    1492            8 :                 // falls through
    1493            8 :             case PipelinePhase.Emit:
    1494            8 :                 return pipelineEmitWithHint;
    1495            8 :             default:
    1496            8 :                 return Debug.assertNever(phase);
    1497            8 :         }
    1498            8 :     }
    1499            8 : 
    1500            8 :     function getNextPipelinePhase(currentPhase: PipelinePhase, emitHint: EmitHint, node: Node) {
    1501            8 :         return getPipelinePhase(currentPhase + 1, emitHint, node);
    1502            8 :     }
    1503            8 : 
    1504            8 :     function pipelineEmitWithNotification(hint: EmitHint, node: Node) {
    1505            8 :         const pipelinePhase = getNextPipelinePhase(PipelinePhase.Notification, hint, node);
    1506            8 :         onEmitNode(hint, node, pipelinePhase);
    1507            8 :     }
    1508            8 : 
    1509            8 :     function pipelineEmitWithHint(hint: EmitHint, node: Node): void {
    1510            8 :         onBeforeEmitNode?.(node);
    1511            8 :         if (preserveSourceNewlines) {
    1512            8 :             const savedPreserveSourceNewlines = preserveSourceNewlines;
    1513            8 :             beforeEmitNode(node);
    1514            8 :             pipelineEmitWithHintWorker(hint, node);
    1515            8 :             afterEmitNode(savedPreserveSourceNewlines);
    1516            8 :         }
    1517            8 :         else {
    1518            8 :             pipelineEmitWithHintWorker(hint, node);
    1519            8 :         }
    1520            8 :         onAfterEmitNode?.(node);
    1521            8 :         // clear the parenthesizer rule as we ascend
    1522            8 :         currentParenthesizerRule = undefined;
    1523            8 :     }
    1524            8 : 
    1525            8 :     function pipelineEmitWithHintWorker(hint: EmitHint, node: Node, allowSnippets = true): void {
    1526            8 :         if (allowSnippets) {
    1527            8 :             const snippet = getSnippetElement(node);
    1528            8 :             if (snippet) {
    1529            8 :                 return emitSnippetNode(hint, node, snippet);
    1530            8 :             }
    1531            8 :         }
    1532            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.SourceFile) return emitSourceFile(cast(node, isSourceFile));
    1533            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.IdentifierName) return emitIdentifier(cast(node, isIdentifier));
    1534            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.JsxAttributeValue) return emitLiteral(cast(node, isStringLiteral), /*jsxAttributeEscape*/ true);
    1535            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.MappedTypeParameter) return emitMappedTypeParameter(cast(node, isTypeParameterDeclaration));
    1536            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.ImportTypeNodeAttributes) return emitImportTypeNodeAttributes(cast(node, isImportAttributes));
    1537            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.EmbeddedStatement) {
    1538            8 :             Debug.assertNode(node, isEmptyStatement);
    1539            8 :             return emitEmptyStatement(/*isEmbeddedStatement*/ true);
    1540            8 :         }
    1541            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.Unspecified) {
    1542            8 :             switch (node.kind) {
    1543            8 :                 // Pseudo-literals
    1544            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TemplateHead:
    1545            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TemplateMiddle:
    1546            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TemplateTail:
    1547            8 :                     return emitLiteral(node as LiteralExpression, /*jsxAttributeEscape*/ false);
    1548            8 : 
    1549            8 :                 // Identifiers
    1550            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.Identifier:
    1551            8 :                     return emitIdentifier(node as Identifier);
    1552            8 : 
    1553            8 :                 // PrivateIdentifiers
    1554            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PrivateIdentifier:
    1555            8 :                     return emitPrivateIdentifier(node as PrivateIdentifier);
    1556            8 : 
    1557            8 :                 // Parse tree nodes
    1558            8 :                 // Names
    1559            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.QualifiedName:
    1560            8 :                     return emitQualifiedName(node as QualifiedName);
    1561            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ComputedPropertyName:
    1562            8 :                     return emitComputedPropertyName(node as ComputedPropertyName);
    1563            8 : 
    1564            8 :                 // Signature elements
    1565            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TypeParameter:
    1566            8 :                     return emitTypeParameter(node as TypeParameterDeclaration);
    1567            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.Parameter:
    1568            8 :                     return emitParameter(node as ParameterDeclaration);
    1569            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.Decorator:
    1570            8 :                     return emitDecorator(node as Decorator);
    1571            8 : 
    1572            8 :                 // Type members
    1573            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PropertySignature:
    1574            8 :                     return emitPropertySignature(node as PropertySignature);
    1575            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PropertyDeclaration:
    1576            8 :                     return emitPropertyDeclaration(node as PropertyDeclaration);
    1577            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.MethodSignature:
    1578            8 :                     return emitMethodSignature(node as MethodSignature);
    1579            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.MethodDeclaration:
    1580            8 :                     return emitMethodDeclaration(node as MethodDeclaration);
    1581            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ClassStaticBlockDeclaration:
    1582            8 :                     return emitClassStaticBlockDeclaration(node as ClassStaticBlockDeclaration);
    1583            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.Constructor:
    1584            8 :                     return emitConstructor(node as ConstructorDeclaration);
    1585            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.GetAccessor:
    1586            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SetAccessor:
    1587            8 :                     return emitAccessorDeclaration(node as AccessorDeclaration);
    1588            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.CallSignature:
    1589            8 :                     return emitCallSignature(node as CallSignatureDeclaration);
    1590            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ConstructSignature:
    1591            8 :                     return emitConstructSignature(node as ConstructSignatureDeclaration);
    1592            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.IndexSignature:
    1593            8 :                     return emitIndexSignature(node as IndexSignatureDeclaration);
    1594            8 :

    1841            8 :                     return;

    1843            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JSDocPublicTag:

    1855            8 :                     return emitJSDocPropertyLikeTag(node as JSDocPropertyLikeTag);

    1862            8 :                     return emitJSDocSimpleTypedTag(node as JSDocTypeTag | JSDocReturnTag | JSDocThisTag | JSDocTypeTag | JSDocThrowsTag | JSDocSatisfiesTag);
    1863            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JSDocTemplateTag:
    1864            8 :                     return emitJSDocTemplateTag(node as JSDocTemplateTag);
    1865            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JSDocTypedefTag:

    1871            8 :                 // SyntaxKind.JSDocPropertyTag (see JSDocParameterTag, above)
    1872            8 : 
    1873            8 :                 // Transformation nodes
    1874            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NotEmittedStatement:
    1875            8 :                     return;
    1876            8 :             }
    1877            8 :             if (isExpression(node)) {
    1878            8 :                 hint = EmitHint.Expression;
    1879            8 :                 if (substituteNode !== noEmitSubstitution) {
    1880            8 :                     const substitute = substituteNode(hint, node) || node;
    1881            8 :                     if (substitute !== node) {
    1882            8 :                         node = substitute;
    1883            8 :                         if (currentParenthesizerRule) {
    1884            8 :                             node = currentParenthesizerRule(node);
    1885            8 :                         }
    1886            8 :                     }
    1887            8 :                 }
    1888            8 :             }
    1889            8 :         }
    1890            8 :         if (hint === EmitHint.Expression) {
    1891            8 :             switch (node.kind) {
    1892            8 :                 // Literals
    1893            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NumericLiteral:
    1894            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.BigIntLiteral:
    1895            8 :                     return emitNumericOrBigIntLiteral(node as NumericLiteral | BigIntLiteral);
    1896            8 : 
    1897            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.StringLiteral:
    1898            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.RegularExpressionLiteral:
    1899            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NoSubstitutionTemplateLiteral:
    1900            8 :                     return emitLiteral(node as LiteralExpression, /*jsxAttributeEscape*/ false);
    1901            8 : 
    1902            8 :                 // Identifiers
    1903            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.Identifier:
    1904            8 :                     return emitIdentifier(node as Identifier);
    1905            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PrivateIdentifier:
    1906            8 :                     return emitPrivateIdentifier(node as PrivateIdentifier);
    1907            8 : 
    1908            8 :                 // Expressions
    1909            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ArrayLiteralExpression:
    1910            8 :                     return emitArrayLiteralExpression(node as ArrayLiteralExpression);
    1911            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ObjectLiteralExpression:
    1912            8 :                     return emitObjectLiteralExpression(node as ObjectLiteralExpression);
    1913            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PropertyAccessExpression:
    1914            8 :                     return emitPropertyAccessExpression(node as PropertyAccessExpression);
    1915            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ElementAccessExpression:
    1916            8 :                     return emitElementAccessExpression(node as ElementAccessExpression);
    1917            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.CallExpression:
    1918            8 :                     return emitCallExpression(node as CallExpression);
    1919            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NewExpression:
    1920            8 :                     return emitNewExpression(node as NewExpression);
    1921            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TaggedTemplateExpression:
    1922            8 :                     return emitTaggedTemplateExpression(node as TaggedTemplateExpression);
    1923            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TypeAssertionExpression:
    1924            8 :                     return emitTypeAssertionExpression(node as TypeAssertion);
    1925            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ParenthesizedExpression:
    1926            8 :                     return emitParenthesizedExpression(node as ParenthesizedExpression);
    1927            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.FunctionExpression:
    1928            8 :                     return emitFunctionExpression(node as FunctionExpression);
    1929            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ArrowFunction:
    1930            8 :                     return emitArrowFunction(node as ArrowFunction);
    1931            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.DeleteExpression:
    1932            8 :                     return emitDeleteExpression(node as DeleteExpression);
    1933            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TypeOfExpression:
    1934            8 :                     return emitTypeOfExpression(node as TypeOfExpression);
    1935            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.VoidExpression:
    1936            8 :                     return emitVoidExpression(node as VoidExpression);
    1937            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.AwaitExpression:
    1938            8 :                     return emitAwaitExpression(node as AwaitExpression);
    1939            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PrefixUnaryExpression:
    1940            8 :                     return emitPrefixUnaryExpression(node as PrefixUnaryExpression);
    1941            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PostfixUnaryExpression:
    1942            8 :                     return emitPostfixUnaryExpression(node as PostfixUnaryExpression);
    1943            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.BinaryExpression:
    1944            8 :                     return emitBinaryExpression(node as BinaryExpression);
    1945            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ConditionalExpression:
    1946            8 :                     return emitConditionalExpression(node as ConditionalExpression);
    1947            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TemplateExpression:
    1948            8 :                     return emitTemplateExpression(node as TemplateExpression);
    1949            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.YieldExpression:
    1950            8 :                     return emitYieldExpression(node as YieldExpression);
    1951            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SpreadElement:
    1952            8 :                     return emitSpreadElement(node as SpreadElement);
    1953            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ClassExpression:
    1954            8 :                     return emitClassExpression(node as ClassExpression);
    1955            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.OmittedExpression:
    1956            8 :                     return;
    1957            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.AsExpression:
    1958            8 :                     return emitAsExpression(node as AsExpression);
    1959            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NonNullExpression:
    1960            8 :                     return emitNonNullExpression(node as NonNullExpression);
    1961            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ExpressionWithTypeArguments:
    1962            8 :                     return emitExpressionWithTypeArguments(node as ExpressionWithTypeArguments);
    1963            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SatisfiesExpression:
    1964            8 :                     return emitSatisfiesExpression(node as SatisfiesExpression);
    1965            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.MetaProperty:
    1966            8 :                     return emitMetaProperty(node as MetaProperty);
    1967            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SyntheticExpression:
    1968            8 :                     return Debug.fail("SyntheticExpression should never be printed.");
    1969            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.MissingDeclaration:
    1970            8 :                     return;
    1971            8 : 
    1972            8 :                 // JSX
    1973            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxElement:
    1974            8 :                     return emitJsxElement(node as JsxElement);
    1975            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxSelfClosingElement:
    1976            8 :                     return emitJsxSelfClosingElement(node as JsxSelfClosingElement);
    1977            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxFragment:
    1978            8 :                     return emitJsxFragment(node as JsxFragment);
    1979            8 : 
    1980            8 :                 // Synthesized list
    1981            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SyntaxList:
    1982            8 :                     return Debug.fail("SyntaxList should not be printed");
    1983            8 : 
    1984            8 :                 // Transformation nodes
    1985            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NotEmittedStatement:
    1986            8 :                     return;
    1987            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PartiallyEmittedExpression:
    1988            8 :                     return emitPartiallyEmittedExpression(node as PartiallyEmittedExpression);
    1989            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.CommaListExpression:
    1990            8 :                     return emitCommaList(node as CommaListExpression);
    1991            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SyntheticReferenceExpression:
    1992            8 :                     return Debug.fail("SyntheticReferenceExpression should not be printed");
    1993            8 :             }
    1994            8 :         }
    1995            8 :         if (isKeyword(node.kind)) return writeTokenNode(node, writeKeyword);
    1996            8 :         if (isTokenKind(node.kind)) return writeTokenNode(node, writePunctuation);
    1997            8 :         Debug.fail(`Unhandled SyntaxKind: ${Debug.formatSyntaxKind(node.kind)}.`);
    1998            8 :     }
    1999            8 : 
    2000            8 :     function emitMappedTypeParameter(node: TypeParameterDeclaration): void {
    2001            8 :         emit(node.name);
    2002            8 :         writeSpace();
    2003            8 :         writeKeyword("in");
    2004            8 :         writeSpace();
    2005            8 :         emit(node.constraint);
    2006            8 :     }
    2007            8 : 
    2008            8 :     function pipelineEmitWithSubstitution(hint: EmitHint, node: Node) {
    2009            8 :         const pipelinePhase = getNextPipelinePhase(PipelinePhase.Substitution, hint, node);
    2010            8 :         Debug.assertIsDefined(lastSubstitution);
    2011            8 :         node = lastSubstitution;
    2012            8 :         lastSubstitution = undefined;
    2013            8 :         pipelinePhase(hint, node);
    2014            8 :     }
    2015            8 : 
    2016            8 :     function emitHelpers(node: Node) {
    2017            8 :         let helpersEmitted = false;
    2018            8 :         const bundle = node.kind === SyntaxKind.Bundle ? node as Bundle : undefined;
    2019            8 :         if (bundle && moduleKind === ModuleKind.None) {
    2020            8 :             return;
    2021            8 :         }
    2022            8 :         const numNodes = bundle ? bundle.sourceFiles.length : 1;
    2023            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < numNodes; i++) {
    2024            8 :             const currentNode = bundle ? bundle.sourceFiles[i] : node;
    2025            8 :             const sourceFile = isSourceFile(currentNode) ? currentNode : currentSourceFile;
    2026            8 :             const shouldSkip = printerOptions.noEmitHelpers || (!!sourceFile && hasRecordedExternalHelpers(sourceFile));
    2027            8 :             const shouldBundle = isSourceFile(currentNode) && !isOwnFileEmit;
    2028            8 :             const helpers = getSortedEmitHelpers(currentNode);
    2029            8 :             if (helpers) {
    2030            8 :                 for (const helper of helpers) {
    2031            8 :                     if (!helper.scoped) {
    2032            8 :                         // Skip the helper if it can be skipped and the noEmitHelpers compiler
    2033            8 :                         // option is set, or if it can be imported and the importHelpers compiler
    2034            8 :                         // option is set.
    2035            8 :                         if (shouldSkip) continue;
    2036            8 : 
    2037            8 :                         // Skip the helper if it can be bundled but hasn't already been emitted and we
    2038            8 :                         // are emitting a bundled module.
    2039            8 :                         if (shouldBundle) {
    2040            8 :                             if (bundledHelpers.get(helper.name)) {
    2041            8 :                                 continue;
    2042            8 :                             }
    2043            8 : 
    2044            8 :                             bundledHelpers.set(helper.name, true);
    2045            8 :                         }
    2046            8 :                     }
    2047            8 :                     else if (bundle) {
    2048            8 :                         // Skip the helper if it is scoped and we are emitting bundled helpers
    2049            8 :                         continue;
    2050            8 :                     }
    2051            8 :                     if (typeof helper.text === "string") {
    2052            8 :                         writeLines(helper.text);
    2053            8 :                     }
    2054            8 :                     else {
    2055            8 :                         writeLines(helper.text(makeFileLevelOptimisticUniqueName));
    2056            8 :                     }
    2057            8 :                     helpersEmitted = true;
    2058            8 :                 }
    2059            8 :             }
    2060            8 :         }
    2061            8 : 
    2062            8 :         return helpersEmitted;
    2063            8 :     }
    2064            8 : 
    2065            8 :     function getSortedEmitHelpers(node: Node) {
    2066            8 :         const helpers = getEmitHelpers(node);
    2067            8 :         return helpers && stableSort(helpers, compareEmitHelpers);
    2068            8 :     }
    2069            8 : 
    2070            8 :     //
    2071            8 :     // Literals/Pseudo-literals
    2072            8 :     //
    2073            8 : 
    2074            8 :     // SyntaxKind.NumericLiteral
    2075            8 :     // SyntaxKind.BigIntLiteral
    2076            8 :     function emitNumericOrBigIntLiteral(node: NumericLiteral | BigIntLiteral) {
    2077            8 :         emitLiteral(node, /*jsxAttributeEscape*/ false);
    2078            8 :     }
    2079            8 : 
    2080            8 :     // SyntaxKind.StringLiteral
    2081            8 :     // SyntaxKind.RegularExpressionLiteral
    2082            8 :     // SyntaxKind.NoSubstitutionTemplateLiteral
    2083            8 :     // SyntaxKind.TemplateHead
    2084            8 :     // SyntaxKind.TemplateMiddle
    2085            8 :     // SyntaxKind.TemplateTail
    2086            8 :     function emitLiteral(node: LiteralLikeNode, jsxAttributeEscape: boolean) {
    2087            8 :         const text = getLiteralTextOfNode(node, printerOptions.neverAsciiEscape, jsxAttributeEscape);
    2088            8 :         if (
    2089            8 :             (printerOptions.sourceMap || printerOptions.inlineSourceMap)
    2090            8 :             && (node.kind === SyntaxKind.StringLiteral || isTemplateLiteralKind(node.kind))
    2091            8 :         ) {
    2092            8 :             writeLiteral(text);
    2093            8 :         }
    2094            8 :         else {
    2095            8 :             // Quick info expects all literals to be called with writeStringLiteral, as there's no specific type for numberLiterals
    2096            8 :             writeStringLiteral(text);
    2097            8 :         }
    2098            8 :     }
    2099            8 : 
    2100            8 :     //
    2101            8 :     // Snippet Elements
    2102            8 :     //
    2103            8 : 
    2104            8 :     function emitSnippetNode(hint: EmitHint, node: Node, snippet: SnippetElement) {
    2105            8 :         switch (snippet.kind) {
    2106            8 :             case SnippetKind.Placeholder:
    2107            8 :                 emitPlaceholder(hint, node, snippet);
    2108            8 :                 break;
    2109            8 :             case SnippetKind.TabStop:
    2110            8 :                 emitTabStop(hint, node, snippet);
    2111            8 :                 break;
    2112            8 :         }
    2113            8 :     }
    2114            8 : 
    2115            8 :     function emitPlaceholder(hint: EmitHint, node: Node, snippet: Placeholder) {
    2116            8 :         nonEscapingWrite(`$\{${snippet.order}:`); // `${2:`
    2117            8 :         pipelineEmitWithHintWorker(hint, node, /*allowSnippets*/ false); // `...`
    2118            8 :         nonEscapingWrite(`}`); // `}`
    2119            8 :         // `${2:...}`
    2120            8 :     }
    2121            8 : 
    2122            8 :     function emitTabStop(hint: EmitHint, node: Node, snippet: TabStop) {
    2123            8 :         // A tab stop should only be attached to an empty node, i.e. a node that doesn't emit any text.
    2124            8 :         Debug.assert(node.kind === SyntaxKind.EmptyStatement, `A tab stop cannot be attached to a node of kind ${Debug.formatSyntaxKind(node.kind)}.`);
    2125            8 :         Debug.assert(hint !== EmitHint.EmbeddedStatement, `A tab stop cannot be attached to an embedded statement.`);
    2126            8 :         nonEscapingWrite(`$${snippet.order}`);
    2127            8 :     }
    2128            8 :

    2133            8 :     function emitIdentifier(node: Identifier) {
    2134            8 :         const writeText = node.symbol ? writeSymbol : write;
    2135            8 :         writeText(getTextOfNode(node, /*includeTrivia*/ false), node.symbol);
    2136            8 :         emitList(node, getIdentifierTypeArguments(node), ListFormat.TypeParameters); // Call emitList directly since it could be an array of TypeParameterDeclarations _or_ type arguments
    2137            8 :     }

    2145            8 :     }

    2153            8 :     function emitEntityName(node: EntityName) {
    2154            8 :         if (node.kind === SyntaxKind.Identifier) {
    2155            8 :             emitExpression(node);
    2156            8 :         }
    2157            8 :         else {
    2158            8 :             emit(node);
    2159            8 :         }
    2160            8 :     }

    2172            8 :     function emitTypeParameter(node: TypeParameterDeclaration) {
    2173            8 :         emitModifierList(node, node.modifiers);
    2174            8 :         emit(node.name);
    2175            8 :         if (node.constraint) {
    2176            8 :             writeSpace();
    2177            8 :             writeKeyword("extends");
    2178            8 :             writeSpace();
    2179            8 :             emit(node.constraint);
    2180            8 :         }
    2181            8 :         if (node.default) {
    2182            8 :             writeSpace();
    2183            8 :             writeOperator("=");
    2184            8 :             writeSpace();
    2185            8 :             emit(node.default);
    2186            8 :         }
    2187            8 :     }
    2188            8 : 
    2189            8 :     function emitParameter(node: ParameterDeclaration) {
    2190            8 :         emitDecoratorsAndModifiers(node, node.modifiers, /*allowDecorators*/ true);
    2191            8 :         emit(node.dotDotDotToken);
    2192            8 :         emitNodeWithWriter(node.name, writeParameter);
    2193            8 :         emit(node.questionToken);
    2194            8 :         if (node.parent && node.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JSDocFunctionType && !node.name) {
    2195            8 :             emit(node.type);
    2196            8 :         }
    2197            8 :         else {
    2198            8 :             emitTypeAnnotation(node.type);
    2199            8 :         }
    2200            8 :         // The comment position has to fallback to any present node within the parameterdeclaration because as it turns out, the parser can make parameter declarations with _just_ an initializer.
    2201            8 :         emitInitializer(node.initializer, node.type ? node.type.end : node.questionToken ? node.questionToken.end : node.name ? node.name.end : node.modifiers ? node.modifiers.end : node.pos, node, parenthesizer.parenthesizeExpressionForDisallowedComma);
    2202            8 :     }
    2203            8 : 
    2204            8 :     function emitDecorator(decorator: Decorator) {
    2205            8 :         writePunctuation("@");
    2206            8 :         emitExpression(decorator.expression, parenthesizer.parenthesizeLeftSideOfAccess);
    2207            8 :     }

    2586            8 :     function emitObjectLiteralExpression(node: ObjectLiteralExpression) {
    2587            8 :         pushNameGenerationScope(node);
    2588            8 :         forEach(node.properties, generateMemberNames);
    2589            8 : 
    2590            8 :         const indentedFlag = getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.Indented;
    2591            8 :         if (indentedFlag) {
    2592            8 :             increaseIndent();
    2593            8 :         }
    2594            8 : 
    2595            8 :         const preferNewLine = node.multiLine ? ListFormat.PreferNewLine : ListFormat.None;
    2596            8 :         const allowTrailingComma = currentSourceFile && currentSourceFile.languageVersion >= ScriptTarget.ES5 && !isJsonSourceFile(currentSourceFile) ? ListFormat.AllowTrailingComma : ListFormat.None;
    2597            8 :         emitList(node, node.properties, ListFormat.ObjectLiteralExpressionProperties | allowTrailingComma | preferNewLine);
    2598            8 : 
    2599            8 :         if (indentedFlag) {
    2600            8 :             decreaseIndent();
    2601            8 :         }
    2602            8 :

    2606            8 :     function emitPropertyAccessExpression(node: PropertyAccessExpression) {
    2607            8 :         emitExpression(node.expression, parenthesizer.parenthesizeLeftSideOfAccess);
    2608            8 :         const token = node.questionDotToken || setTextRangePosEnd(factory.createToken(SyntaxKind.DotToken) as DotToken, node.expression.end, node.name.pos);
    2609            8 :         const linesBeforeDot = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.expression, token);
    2610            8 :         const linesAfterDot = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, token, node.name);
    2611            8 : 
    2612            8 :         writeLinesAndIndent(linesBeforeDot, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ false);
    2613            8 : 
    2614            8 :         const shouldEmitDotDot = token.kind !== SyntaxKind.QuestionDotToken &&
    2615            8 :             mayNeedDotDotForPropertyAccess(node.expression) &&
    2616            8 :             !writer.hasTrailingComment() &&
    2617            8 :             !writer.hasTrailingWhitespace();
    2618            8 : 
    2619            8 :         if (shouldEmitDotDot) {
    2620            8 :             writePunctuation(".");
    2621            8 :         }
    2622            8 : 
    2623            8 :         if (node.questionDotToken) {
    2624            8 :             emit(token);
    2625            8 :         }
    2626            8 :         else {
    2627            8 :             emitTokenWithComment(token.kind, node.expression.end, writePunctuation, node);
    2628            8 :         }
    2629            8 :         writeLinesAndIndent(linesAfterDot, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ false);
    2630            8 :         emit(node.name);
    2631            8 :         decreaseIndentIf(linesBeforeDot, linesAfterDot);
    2632            8 :     }
    2633            8 : 
    2634            8 :     // 1..toString is a valid property access, emit a dot after the literal
    2635            8 :     // Also emit a dot if expression is a integer const enum value - it will appear in generated code as numeric literal
    2636            8 :     function mayNeedDotDotForPropertyAccess(expression: Expression) {
    2637            8 :         expression = skipPartiallyEmittedExpressions(expression);
    2638            8 :         if (isNumericLiteral(expression)) {
    2639            8 :             // check if numeric literal is a decimal literal that was originally written with a dot
    2640            8 :             const text = getLiteralTextOfNode(expression as LiteralExpression, /*neverAsciiEscape*/ true, /*jsxAttributeEscape*/ false);
    2641            8 :             // If the number will be printed verbatim and it doesn't already contain a dot or an exponent indicator, add one
    2642            8 :             // if the expression doesn't have any comments that will be emitted.
    2643            8 :             return !(expression.numericLiteralFlags & TokenFlags.WithSpecifier)
    2644            8 :                 && !text.includes(tokenToString(SyntaxKind.DotToken))
    2645            8 :                 && !text.includes(String.fromCharCode(CharacterCodes.E))
    2646            8 :                 && !text.includes(String.fromCharCode(CharacterCodes.e));
    2647            8 :         }
    2648            8 :         else if (isAccessExpression(expression)) {
    2649            8 :             // check if constant enum value is a non-negative integer
    2650            8 :             const constantValue = getConstantValue(expression);
    2651            8 :             // isFinite handles cases when constantValue is undefined
    2652            8 :             return typeof constantValue === "number" && isFinite(constantValue)
    2653            8 :                 && constantValue >= 0 && Math.floor(constantValue) === constantValue;
    2654            8 :         }
    2655            8 :     }
    2656            8 : 
    2657            8 :     function emitElementAccessExpression(node: ElementAccessExpression) {
    2658            8 :         emitExpression(node.expression, parenthesizer.parenthesizeLeftSideOfAccess);
    2659            8 :         emit(node.questionDotToken);
    2660            8 :         emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.OpenBracketToken, node.expression.end, writePunctuation, node);
    2661            8 :         emitExpression(node.argumentExpression);
    2662            8 :         emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.CloseBracketToken, node.argumentExpression.end, writePunctuation, node);
    2663            8 :     }
