    2775            8 :     function emitPrefixUnaryExpression(node: PrefixUnaryExpression) {
    2776            8 :         writeTokenText(node.operator, writeOperator);
    2777            8 :         if (shouldEmitWhitespaceBeforeOperand(node)) {
    2778            8 :             writeSpace();
    2779            8 :         }
    2780            8 :         emitExpression(node.operand, parenthesizer.parenthesizeOperandOfPrefixUnary);
    2781            8 :     }
    2782            8 : 
    2783            8 :     function shouldEmitWhitespaceBeforeOperand(node: PrefixUnaryExpression) {
    2784            8 :         // In some cases, we need to emit a space between the operator and the operand. One obvious case
    2785            8 :         // is when the operator is an identifier, like delete or typeof. We also need to do this for plus
    2786            8 :         // and minus expressions in certain cases. Specifically, consider the following two cases (parens
    2787            8 :         // are just for clarity of exposition, and not part of the source code):
    2788            8 :         //
    2789            8 :         //  (+(+1))
    2790            8 :         //  (+(++1))
    2791            8 :         //
    2792            8 :         // We need to emit a space in both cases. In the first case, the absence of a space will make
    2793            8 :         // the resulting expression a prefix increment operation. And in the second, it will make the resulting
    2794            8 :         // expression a prefix increment whose operand is a plus expression - (++(+x))
    2795            8 :         // The same is true of minus of course.
    2796            8 :         const operand = node.operand;
    2797            8 :         return operand.kind === SyntaxKind.PrefixUnaryExpression
    2798            8 :             && ((node.operator === SyntaxKind.PlusToken && ((operand as PrefixUnaryExpression).operator === SyntaxKind.PlusToken || (operand as PrefixUnaryExpression).operator === SyntaxKind.PlusPlusToken))
    2799            8 :                 || (node.operator === SyntaxKind.MinusToken && ((operand as PrefixUnaryExpression).operator === SyntaxKind.MinusToken || (operand as PrefixUnaryExpression).operator === SyntaxKind.MinusMinusToken)));
    2800            8 :     }
    2801            8 : 
    2802            8 :     function emitPostfixUnaryExpression(node: PostfixUnaryExpression) {
    2803            8 :         emitExpression(node.operand, parenthesizer.parenthesizeOperandOfPostfixUnary);
    2804            8 :         writeTokenText(node.operator, writeOperator);
    2805            8 :     }
    2806            8 : 
    2807            8 :     function createEmitBinaryExpression() {
    2808            8 :         interface WorkArea {
    2809            8 :             stackIndex: number;
    2810            8 :             preserveSourceNewlinesStack: (boolean | undefined)[];
    2811            8 :             containerPosStack: number[];
    2812            8 :             containerEndStack: number[];
    2813            8 :             declarationListContainerEndStack: number[];
    2814            8 :             shouldEmitCommentsStack: boolean[];
    2815            8 :             shouldEmitSourceMapsStack: boolean[];
    2816            8 :         }
    2817            8 : 
    2818            8 :         return createBinaryExpressionTrampoline(onEnter, onLeft, onOperator, onRight, onExit, /*foldState*/ undefined);
    2819            8 : 
    2820            8 :         function onEnter(node: BinaryExpression, state: WorkArea | undefined) {
    2821            8 :             if (state) {
    2822            8 :                 state.stackIndex++;
    2823            8 :                 state.preserveSourceNewlinesStack[state.stackIndex] = preserveSourceNewlines;
    2824            8 :                 state.containerPosStack[state.stackIndex] = containerPos;
    2825            8 :                 state.containerEndStack[state.stackIndex] = containerEnd;
    2826            8 :                 state.declarationListContainerEndStack[state.stackIndex] = declarationListContainerEnd;
    2827            8 :                 const emitComments = state.shouldEmitCommentsStack[state.stackIndex] = shouldEmitComments(node);
    2828            8 :                 const emitSourceMaps = state.shouldEmitSourceMapsStack[state.stackIndex] = shouldEmitSourceMaps(node);
    2829            8 :                 onBeforeEmitNode?.(node);
    2830            8 :                 if (emitComments) emitCommentsBeforeNode(node);
    2831            8 :                 if (emitSourceMaps) emitSourceMapsBeforeNode(node);
    2832            8 :                 beforeEmitNode(node);
    2833            8 :             }
    2834            8 :             else {
    2835            8 :                 state = {
    2836            8 :                     stackIndex: 0,
    2837            8 :                     preserveSourceNewlinesStack: [undefined],
    2838            8 :                     containerPosStack: [-1],
    2839            8 :                     containerEndStack: [-1],
    2840            8 :                     declarationListContainerEndStack: [-1],
    2841            8 :                     shouldEmitCommentsStack: [false],
    2842            8 :                     shouldEmitSourceMapsStack: [false],
    2843            8 :                 };
    2844            8 :             }
    2845            8 :             return state;
    2846            8 :         }
    2847            8 : 
    2848            8 :         function onLeft(next: Expression, _workArea: WorkArea, parent: BinaryExpression) {
    2849            8 :             return maybeEmitExpression(next, parent, "left");
    2850            8 :         }
    2851            8 : 
    2852            8 :         function onOperator(operatorToken: BinaryOperatorToken, _state: WorkArea, node: BinaryExpression) {
    2853            8 :             const isCommaOperator = operatorToken.kind !== SyntaxKind.CommaToken;
    2854            8 :             const linesBeforeOperator = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.left, operatorToken);
    2855            8 :             const linesAfterOperator = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, operatorToken, node.right);
    2856            8 :             writeLinesAndIndent(linesBeforeOperator, isCommaOperator);
    2857            8 :             emitLeadingCommentsOfPosition(operatorToken.pos);
    2858            8 :             writeTokenNode(operatorToken, operatorToken.kind === SyntaxKind.InKeyword ? writeKeyword : writeOperator);
    2859            8 :             emitTrailingCommentsOfPosition(operatorToken.end, /*prefixSpace*/ true); // Binary operators should have a space before the comment starts
    2860            8 :             writeLinesAndIndent(linesAfterOperator, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ true);
    2861            8 :         }
    2862            8 : 
    2863            8 :         function onRight(next: Expression, _workArea: WorkArea, parent: BinaryExpression) {
    2864            8 :             return maybeEmitExpression(next, parent, "right");
    2865            8 :         }
    2866            8 : 
    2867            8 :         function onExit(node: BinaryExpression, state: WorkArea) {
    2868            8 :             const linesBeforeOperator = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.left, node.operatorToken);
    2869            8 :             const linesAfterOperator = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.operatorToken, node.right);
    2870            8 :             decreaseIndentIf(linesBeforeOperator, linesAfterOperator);
    2871            8 :             if (state.stackIndex > 0) {
    2872            8 :                 const savedPreserveSourceNewlines = state.preserveSourceNewlinesStack[state.stackIndex];
    2873            8 :                 const savedContainerPos = state.containerPosStack[state.stackIndex];
    2874            8 :                 const savedContainerEnd = state.containerEndStack[state.stackIndex];
    2875            8 :                 const savedDeclarationListContainerEnd = state.declarationListContainerEndStack[state.stackIndex];
    2876            8 :                 const shouldEmitComments = state.shouldEmitCommentsStack[state.stackIndex];
    2877            8 :                 const shouldEmitSourceMaps = state.shouldEmitSourceMapsStack[state.stackIndex];
    2878            8 :                 afterEmitNode(savedPreserveSourceNewlines);
    2879            8 :                 if (shouldEmitSourceMaps) emitSourceMapsAfterNode(node);
    2880            8 :                 if (shouldEmitComments) emitCommentsAfterNode(node, savedContainerPos, savedContainerEnd, savedDeclarationListContainerEnd);
    2881            8 :                 onAfterEmitNode?.(node);
    2882            8 :                 state.stackIndex--;
    2883            8 :             }
    2884            8 :         }
    2885            8 : 
    2886            8 :         function maybeEmitExpression(next: Expression, parent: BinaryExpression, side: "left" | "right") {
    2887            8 :             const parenthesizerRule = side === "left" ?
    2888            8 :                 parenthesizer.getParenthesizeLeftSideOfBinaryForOperator(parent.operatorToken.kind) :
    2889            8 :                 parenthesizer.getParenthesizeRightSideOfBinaryForOperator(parent.operatorToken.kind);
    2890            8 : 
    2891            8 :             let pipelinePhase = getPipelinePhase(PipelinePhase.Notification, EmitHint.Expression, next);
    2892            8 :             if (pipelinePhase === pipelineEmitWithSubstitution) {
    2893            8 :                 Debug.assertIsDefined(lastSubstitution);
    2894            8 :                 next = parenthesizerRule(cast(lastSubstitution, isExpression));
    2895            8 :                 pipelinePhase = getNextPipelinePhase(PipelinePhase.Substitution, EmitHint.Expression, next);
    2896            8 :                 lastSubstitution = undefined;
    2897            8 :             }
    2898            8 : 
    2899            8 :             if (
    2900            8 :                 pipelinePhase === pipelineEmitWithComments ||
    2901            8 :                 pipelinePhase === pipelineEmitWithSourceMaps ||
    2902            8 :                 pipelinePhase === pipelineEmitWithHint
    2903            8 :             ) {
    2904            8 :                 if (isBinaryExpression(next)) {
    2905            8 :                     return next;
    2906            8 :                 }
    2907            8 :             }
    2908            8 : 
    2909            8 :             currentParenthesizerRule = parenthesizerRule;
    2910            8 :             pipelinePhase(EmitHint.Expression, next);
    2911            8 :         }
    2912            8 :     }
    2913            8 : 
    2914            8 :     function emitConditionalExpression(node: ConditionalExpression) {
    2915            8 :         const linesBeforeQuestion = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.condition, node.questionToken);
    2916            8 :         const linesAfterQuestion = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.questionToken, node.whenTrue);
    2917            8 :         const linesBeforeColon = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.whenTrue, node.colonToken);
    2918            8 :         const linesAfterColon = getLinesBetweenNodes(node, node.colonToken, node.whenFalse);
    2919            8 : 
    2920            8 :         emitExpression(node.condition, parenthesizer.parenthesizeConditionOfConditionalExpression);
    2921            8 :         writeLinesAndIndent(linesBeforeQuestion, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ true);
    2922            8 :         emit(node.questionToken);
    2923            8 :         writeLinesAndIndent(linesAfterQuestion, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ true);
    2924            8 :         emitExpression(node.whenTrue, parenthesizer.parenthesizeBranchOfConditionalExpression);
    2925            8 :         decreaseIndentIf(linesBeforeQuestion, linesAfterQuestion);
    2926            8 : 
    2927            8 :         writeLinesAndIndent(linesBeforeColon, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ true);
    2928            8 :         emit(node.colonToken);
    2929            8 :         writeLinesAndIndent(linesAfterColon, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ true);
    2930            8 :         emitExpression(node.whenFalse, parenthesizer.parenthesizeBranchOfConditionalExpression);
    2931            8 :         decreaseIndentIf(linesBeforeColon, linesAfterColon);
    2932            8 :     }

    3004            8 :     function emitBlock(node: Block) {
    3005            8 :         emitBlockStatements(node, /*forceSingleLine*/ !node.multiLine && isEmptyBlock(node));

    3007            8 : 
    3008            8 :     function emitBlockStatements(node: BlockLike, forceSingleLine: boolean) {
    3009            8 :         emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken, node.pos, writePunctuation, /*contextNode*/ node);
    3010            8 :         const format = forceSingleLine || getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.SingleLine ? ListFormat.SingleLineBlockStatements : ListFormat.MultiLineBlockStatements;
    3011            8 :         emitList(node, node.statements, format);
    3012            8 :         emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.CloseBraceToken, node.statements.end, writePunctuation, /*contextNode*/ node, /*indentLeading*/ !!(format & ListFormat.MultiLine));
    3013            8 :     }

    3015            8 :     function emitVariableStatement(node: VariableStatement) {
    3016            8 :         emitDecoratorsAndModifiers(node, node.modifiers, /*allowDecorators*/ false);

    3020            8 : 
    3021            8 :     function emitEmptyStatement(isEmbeddedStatement: boolean) {
    3022            8 :         // While most trailing semicolons are possibly insignificant, an embedded "empty"
    3023            8 :         // statement is significant and cannot be elided by a trailing-semicolon-omitting writer.
    3024            8 :         if (isEmbeddedStatement) {
    3025            8 :             writePunctuation(";");
    3026            8 :         }
    3027            8 :         else {
    3028            8 :             writeTrailingSemicolon();
    3029            8 :         }
    3030            8 :     }

    3032            8 :     function emitExpressionStatement(node: ExpressionStatement) {
    3033            8 :         emitExpression(node.expression, parenthesizer.parenthesizeExpressionOfExpressionStatement);
    3034            8 :         // Emit semicolon in non json files
    3035            8 :         // or if json file that created synthesized expression(eg.define expression statement when --out and amd code generation)
    3036            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile || !isJsonSourceFile(currentSourceFile) || nodeIsSynthesized(node.expression)) {
    3037            8 :             writeTrailingSemicolon();
    3038            8 :         }
    3039            8 :     }

    3041            8 :     function emitIfStatement(node: IfStatement) {
    3042            8 :         const openParenPos = emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.IfKeyword, node.pos, writeKeyword, node);
    3043            8 :         writeSpace();

    3045            8 :         emitExpression(node.expression);
    3046            8 :         emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.CloseParenToken, node.expression.end, writePunctuation, node);
    3047            8 :         emitEmbeddedStatement(node, node.thenStatement);

    3049            8 :             writeLineOrSpace(node, node.thenStatement, node.elseStatement);
    3050            8 :             emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.ElseKeyword, node.thenStatement.end, writeKeyword, node);
    3051            8 :             if (node.elseStatement.kind === SyntaxKind.IfStatement) {
    3052            8 :                 writeSpace();
    3053            8 :                 emit(node.elseStatement);
    3054            8 :             }
    3055            8 :             else {
    3056            8 :                 emitEmbeddedStatement(node, node.elseStatement);
    3057            8 :             }
    3058            8 :         }
    3059            8 :     }

    3074            8 :         }

    3076            8 :             writeLineOrSpace(node, node.statement, node.expression);
    3077            8 :         }
    3078            8 :

    3088            8 :     function emitForStatement(node: ForStatement) {

    3092            8 :         emitForBinding(node.initializer);
    3093            8 :         pos = emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.SemicolonToken, node.initializer ? node.initializer.end : pos, writePunctuation, node);
    3094            8 :         emitExpressionWithLeadingSpace(node.condition);

    3096            8 :         emitExpressionWithLeadingSpace(node.incrementor);
    3097            8 :         emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.CloseParenToken, node.incrementor ? node.incrementor.end : pos, writePunctuation, node);
    3098            8 :         emitEmbeddedStatement(node, node.statement);
    3099            8 :     }

    3150            8 : 
    3151            8 :     function emitTokenWithComment(token: SyntaxKind, pos: number, writer: (s: string) => void, contextNode: Node, indentLeading?: boolean) {
    3152            8 :         const node = getParseTreeNode(contextNode);
    3153            8 :         const isSimilarNode = node && node.kind === contextNode.kind;
    3154            8 :         const startPos = pos;
    3155            8 :         if (isSimilarNode && currentSourceFile) {
    3156            8 :             pos = skipTrivia(currentSourceFile.text, pos);
    3157            8 :         }
    3158            8 :         if (isSimilarNode && contextNode.pos !== startPos) {
    3159            8 :             const needsIndent = indentLeading && currentSourceFile && !positionsAreOnSameLine(startPos, pos, currentSourceFile);
    3160            8 :             if (needsIndent) {
    3161            8 :                 increaseIndent();
    3162            8 :             }
    3163            8 :             emitLeadingCommentsOfPosition(startPos);
    3164            8 :             if (needsIndent) {
    3165            8 :                 decreaseIndent();
    3166            8 :             }
    3167            8 :         }
    3168            8 : 
    3169            8 :         // We don't emit source positions for most tokens as it tends to be quite noisy, however
    3170            8 :         // we need to emit source positions for open and close braces so that tools like istanbul
    3171            8 :         // can map branches for code coverage. However, we still omit brace source positions when
    3172            8 :         // the output is a declaration file.
    3173            8 :         if (!omitBraceSourcePositions && (token === SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken || token === SyntaxKind.CloseBraceToken)) {
    3174            8 :             pos = writeToken(token, pos, writer, contextNode);
    3175            8 :         }
    3176            8 :         else {
    3177            8 :             pos = writeTokenText(token, writer, pos);
    3178            8 :         }
    3179            8 : 
    3180            8 :         if (isSimilarNode && contextNode.end !== pos) {
    3181            8 :             const isJsxExprContext = contextNode.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxExpression;
    3182            8 :             emitTrailingCommentsOfPosition(pos, /*prefixSpace*/ !isJsxExprContext, /*forceNoNewline*/ isJsxExprContext);
    3183            8 :         }
    3184            8 :         return pos;
    3185            8 :     }
    3186            8 : 
    3187            8 :     function commentWillEmitNewLine(node: CommentRange) {
    3188            8 :         return node.kind === SyntaxKind.SingleLineCommentTrivia || !!node.hasTrailingNewLine;
    3189            8 :     }
    3190            8 : 
    3191            8 :     function willEmitLeadingNewLine(node: Expression): boolean {
    3192            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile) return false;
    3193            8 :         const leadingCommentRanges = getLeadingCommentRanges(currentSourceFile.text, node.pos);
    3194            8 :         if (leadingCommentRanges) {
    3195            8 :             const parseNode = getParseTreeNode(node);
    3196            8 :             if (parseNode && isParenthesizedExpression(parseNode.parent)) {
    3197            8 :                 return true;
    3198            8 :             }
    3199            8 :         }
    3200            8 :         if (some(leadingCommentRanges, commentWillEmitNewLine)) return true;
    3201            8 :         if (some(getSyntheticLeadingComments(node), commentWillEmitNewLine)) return true;
    3202            8 :         if (isPartiallyEmittedExpression(node)) {
    3203            8 :             if (node.pos !== node.expression.pos) {
    3204            8 :                 if (some(getTrailingCommentRanges(currentSourceFile.text, node.expression.pos), commentWillEmitNewLine)) return true;
    3205            8 :             }
    3206            8 :             return willEmitLeadingNewLine(node.expression);
    3207            8 :         }
    3208            8 :         return false;
    3209            8 :     }
    3210            8 : 
    3211            8 :     /**
    3212            8 :      * Wraps an expression in parens if we would emit a leading comment that would introduce a line separator
    3213            8 :      * between the node and its parent.
    3214            8 :      */
    3215            8 :     function parenthesizeExpressionForNoAsi(node: Expression) {
    3216            8 :         if (!commentsDisabled && isPartiallyEmittedExpression(node) && willEmitLeadingNewLine(node)) {
    3217            8 :             const parseNode = getParseTreeNode(node);
    3218            8 :             if (parseNode && isParenthesizedExpression(parseNode)) {
    3219            8 :                 // If the original node was a parenthesized expression, restore it to preserve comment and source map emit
    3220            8 :                 const parens = factory.createParenthesizedExpression(node.expression);
    3221            8 :                 setOriginalNode(parens, node);
    3222            8 :                 setTextRange(parens, parseNode);
    3223            8 :                 return parens;
    3224            8 :             }
    3225            8 :             return factory.createParenthesizedExpression(node);
    3226            8 :         }
    3227            8 :         return node;
    3228            8 :     }
    3229            8 : 
    3230            8 :     function parenthesizeExpressionForNoAsiAndDisallowedComma(node: Expression) {
    3231            8 :         return parenthesizeExpressionForNoAsi(parenthesizer.parenthesizeExpressionForDisallowedComma(node));
    3232            8 :     }
    3233            8 :

    3236            8 :         emitExpressionWithLeadingSpace(node.expression && parenthesizeExpressionForNoAsi(node.expression), parenthesizeExpressionForNoAsi);
    3237            8 :         writeTrailingSemicolon();

    3282            8 :             emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.FinallyKeyword, (node.catchClause || node.tryBlock).end, writeKeyword, node);

    3290            8 :         writeTrailingSemicolon();

    3292            8 :

    3297            8 :     function emitVariableDeclaration(node: VariableDeclaration) {

    3302            8 :     }
    3303            8 : 
    3304            8 :     function emitVariableDeclarationList(node: VariableDeclarationList) {
    3305            8 :         if (isVarAwaitUsing(node)) {
    3306            8 :             writeKeyword("await");
    3307            8 :             writeSpace();

    3309            8 :         }
    3310            8 :         else {
    3311            8 :             const head = isLet(node) ? "let" :
    3312            8 :                 isVarConst(node) ? "const" :
    3313            8 :                 isVarUsing(node) ? "using" :
    3314            8 :                 "var";
    3315            8 :             writeKeyword(head);

    3321            8 :     function emitFunctionDeclaration(node: FunctionDeclaration) {
    3322            8 :         emitFunctionDeclarationOrExpression(node);
    3323            8 :     }
    3324            8 : 
    3325            8 :     function emitFunctionDeclarationOrExpression(node: FunctionDeclaration | FunctionExpression) {
    3326            8 :         emitDecoratorsAndModifiers(node, node.modifiers, /*allowDecorators*/ false);
    3327            8 :         writeKeyword("function");
    3328            8 :         emit(node.asteriskToken);
    3329            8 :         writeSpace();
    3330            8 :         emitIdentifierName(node.name);
    3331            8 :         emitSignatureAndBody(node, emitSignatureHead, emitFunctionBody);
    3332            8 :     }
    3333            8 : 
    3334            8 :     function emitSignatureAndBody<T extends SignatureDeclaration>(node: T, emitSignatureHead: (node: T) => void, emitBody: (node: T) => void) {
    3335            8 :         const indentedFlag = getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.Indented;
    3336            8 :         if (indentedFlag) {
    3337            8 :             increaseIndent();
    3338            8 :         }
    3339            8 : 
    3340            8 :         pushNameGenerationScope(node);
    3341            8 :         forEach(node.parameters, generateNames);
    3342            8 :         emitSignatureHead(node);
    3343            8 :         emitBody(node);
    3344            8 :         popNameGenerationScope(node);
    3345            8 : 
    3346            8 :         if (indentedFlag) {
    3347            8 :             decreaseIndent();
    3348            8 :         }
    3349            8 :     }
    3350            8 : 
    3351            8 :     function emitFunctionBody<T extends Exclude<FunctionLikeDeclaration, ArrowFunction>>(node: T) {
    3352            8 :         const body = node.body;
    3353            8 :         if (body) {
    3354            8 :             emitBlockFunctionBody(body);
    3355            8 :         }
    3356            8 :         else {
    3357            8 :             writeTrailingSemicolon();
    3358            8 :         }
    3359            8 :     }
    3360            8 : 
    3361            8 :     function emitEmptyFunctionBody(_node: SignatureDeclaration) {
    3362            8 :         writeTrailingSemicolon();
    3363            8 :     }
    3364            8 : 
    3365            8 :     function emitSignatureHead(node: SignatureDeclaration) {
    3366            8 :         emitTypeParameters(node, node.typeParameters);
    3367            8 :         emitParameters(node, node.parameters);
    3368            8 :         emitTypeAnnotation(node.type);
    3369            8 :     }
    3370            8 : 
    3371            8 :     function shouldEmitBlockFunctionBodyOnSingleLine(body: Block) {
    3372            8 :         // We must emit a function body as a single-line body in the following case:
    3373            8 :         // * The body has NodeEmitFlags.SingleLine specified.
    3374            8 : 
    3375            8 :         // We must emit a function body as a multi-line body in the following cases:
    3376            8 :         // * The body is explicitly marked as multi-line.
    3377            8 :         // * A non-synthesized body's start and end position are on different lines.
    3378            8 :         // * Any statement in the body starts on a new line.
    3379            8 : 
    3380            8 :         if (getEmitFlags(body) & EmitFlags.SingleLine) {
    3381            8 :             return true;
    3382            8 :         }
    3383            8 : 
    3384            8 :         if (body.multiLine) {
    3385            8 :             return false;
    3386            8 :         }
    3387            8 : 
    3388            8 :         if (!nodeIsSynthesized(body) && currentSourceFile && !rangeIsOnSingleLine(body, currentSourceFile)) {
    3389            8 :             return false;
    3390            8 :         }
    3391            8 : 
    3392            8 :         if (
    3393            8 :             getLeadingLineTerminatorCount(body, firstOrUndefined(body.statements), ListFormat.PreserveLines)
    3394            8 :             || getClosingLineTerminatorCount(body, lastOrUndefined(body.statements), ListFormat.PreserveLines, body.statements)
    3395            8 :         ) {
    3396            8 :             return false;
    3397            8 :         }
    3398            8 : 
    3399            8 :         let previousStatement: Statement | undefined;
    3400            8 :         for (const statement of body.statements) {
    3401            8 :             if (getSeparatingLineTerminatorCount(previousStatement, statement, ListFormat.PreserveLines) > 0) {
    3402            8 :                 return false;
    3403            8 :             }
    3404            8 : 
    3405            8 :             previousStatement = statement;
    3406            8 :         }
    3407            8 : 
    3408            8 :         return true;
    3409            8 :     }
    3410            8 : 
    3411            8 :     function emitBlockFunctionBody(body: Block) {
    3412            8 :         generateNames(body);
    3413            8 :         onBeforeEmitNode?.(body);
    3414            8 :         writeSpace();
    3415            8 :         writePunctuation("{");
    3416            8 :         increaseIndent();
    3417            8 : 
    3418            8 :         const emitBlockFunctionBody = shouldEmitBlockFunctionBodyOnSingleLine(body)
    3419            8 :             ? emitBlockFunctionBodyOnSingleLine
    3420            8 :             : emitBlockFunctionBodyWorker;
    3421            8 : 
    3422            8 :         emitBodyWithDetachedComments(body, body.statements, emitBlockFunctionBody);
    3423            8 : 
    3424            8 :         decreaseIndent();
    3425            8 :         writeToken(SyntaxKind.CloseBraceToken, body.statements.end, writePunctuation, body);
    3426            8 :         onAfterEmitNode?.(body);
    3427            8 :     }
    3428            8 : 
    3429            8 :     function emitBlockFunctionBodyOnSingleLine(body: Block) {
    3430            8 :         emitBlockFunctionBodyWorker(body, /*emitBlockFunctionBodyOnSingleLine*/ true);
    3431            8 :     }
    3432            8 : 
    3433            8 :     function emitBlockFunctionBodyWorker(body: Block, emitBlockFunctionBodyOnSingleLine?: boolean) {
    3434            8 :         // Emit all the prologue directives (like "use strict").
    3435            8 :         const statementOffset = emitPrologueDirectives(body.statements);
    3436            8 :         const pos = writer.getTextPos();
    3437            8 :         emitHelpers(body);
    3438            8 :         if (statementOffset === 0 && pos === writer.getTextPos() && emitBlockFunctionBodyOnSingleLine) {
    3439            8 :             decreaseIndent();
    3440            8 :             emitList(body, body.statements, ListFormat.SingleLineFunctionBodyStatements);
    3441            8 :             increaseIndent();
    3442            8 :         }
    3443            8 :         else {
    3444            8 :             emitList(body, body.statements, ListFormat.MultiLineFunctionBodyStatements, /*parenthesizerRule*/ undefined, statementOffset);
    3445            8 :         }
    3446            8 :     }
    3447            8 : 
    3448            8 :     function emitClassDeclaration(node: ClassDeclaration) {

    3452            8 :     function emitClassDeclarationOrExpression(node: ClassDeclaration | ClassExpression) {
    3453            8 :         emitDecoratorsAndModifiers(node, node.modifiers, /*allowDecorators*/ true);
    3454            8 :         emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.ClassKeyword, moveRangePastModifiers(node).pos, writeKeyword, node);
    3455            8 :         if (node.name) {
    3456            8 :             writeSpace();
    3457            8 :             emitIdentifierName(node.name);
    3458            8 :         }
    3459            8 : 
    3460            8 :         const indentedFlag = getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.Indented;
    3461            8 :         if (indentedFlag) {
    3462            8 :             increaseIndent();
    3463            8 :         }
    3464            8 : 
    3465            8 :         emitTypeParameters(node, node.typeParameters);
    3466            8 :         emitList(node, node.heritageClauses, ListFormat.ClassHeritageClauses);
    3467            8 :         writeSpace();
    3468            8 :         writePunctuation("{");
    3469            8 : 
    3470            8 :         pushNameGenerationScope(node);
    3471            8 :         forEach(node.members, generateMemberNames);
    3472            8 :         emitList(node, node.members, ListFormat.ClassMembers);
    3473            8 :         popNameGenerationScope(node);
    3474            8 : 
    3475            8 :         writePunctuation("}");
    3476            8 : 
    3477            8 :         if (indentedFlag) {
    3478            8 :             decreaseIndent();
    3479            8 :         }
    3480            8 :     }

    3629            8 :     function emitExportAssignment(node: ExportAssignment) {
    3630            8 :         const nextPos = emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.ExportKeyword, node.pos, writeKeyword, node);
    3631            8 :         writeSpace();
    3632            8 :         if (node.isExportEquals) {
    3633            8 :             emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.EqualsToken, nextPos, writeOperator, node);
    3634            8 :         }
    3635            8 :         else {
    3636            8 :             emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.DefaultKeyword, nextPos, writeKeyword, node);
    3637            8 :         }
    3638            8 :         writeSpace();
    3639            8 :         emitExpression(
    3640            8 :             node.expression,
    3641            8 :             node.isExportEquals ?
    3642            8 :                 parenthesizer.getParenthesizeRightSideOfBinaryForOperator(SyntaxKind.EqualsToken) :
    3643            8 :                 parenthesizer.parenthesizeExpressionOfExportDefault,
    3644            8 :         );

    3838            8 :     function hasTrailingCommentsAtPosition(pos: number) {
    3839            8 :         let result = false;
    3840            8 :         forEachTrailingCommentRange(currentSourceFile?.text || "", pos + 1, () => result = true);
    3841            8 :         return result;
    3842            8 :     }
    3843            8 : 
    3844            8 :     function hasLeadingCommentsAtPosition(pos: number) {
    3845            8 :         let result = false;
    3846            8 :         forEachLeadingCommentRange(currentSourceFile?.text || "", pos + 1, () => result = true);
    3847            8 :         return result;
    3848            8 :     }
    3849            8 : 
    3850            8 :     function hasCommentsAtPosition(pos: number) {
    3851            8 :         return hasTrailingCommentsAtPosition(pos) || hasLeadingCommentsAtPosition(pos);
    3852            8 :     }
    3853            8 : 
    3854            8 :     function emitJsxExpression(node: JsxExpression) {
    3855            8 :         if (node.expression || (!commentsDisabled && !nodeIsSynthesized(node) && hasCommentsAtPosition(node.pos))) { // preserve empty expressions if they contain comments!
    3856            8 :             const isMultiline = currentSourceFile && !nodeIsSynthesized(node) && getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(currentSourceFile, node.pos).line !== getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(currentSourceFile, node.end).line;
    3857            8 :             if (isMultiline) {
    3858            8 :                 writer.increaseIndent();
    3859            8 :             }
    3860            8 :             const end = emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken, node.pos, writePunctuation, node);
    3861            8 :             emit(node.dotDotDotToken);
    3862            8 :             emitExpression(node.expression);
    3863            8 :             emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.CloseBraceToken, node.expression?.end || end, writePunctuation, node);
    3864            8 :             if (isMultiline) {
    3865            8 :                 writer.decreaseIndent();
    3866            8 :             }
    3867            8 :         }
    3868            8 :     }

    3899            8 :         emitCaseOrDefaultClauseRest(node, node.statements, pos);

    3902            8 :     function emitCaseOrDefaultClauseRest(parentNode: Node, statements: NodeArray<Statement>, colonPos: number) {
    3903            8 :         const emitAsSingleStatement = statements.length === 1 &&
    3904            8 :             (
    3905            8 :                 // treat synthesized nodes as located on the same line for emit purposes
    3906            8 :                 !currentSourceFile ||
    3907            8 :                 nodeIsSynthesized(parentNode) ||
    3908            8 :                 nodeIsSynthesized(statements[0]) ||
    3909            8 :                 rangeStartPositionsAreOnSameLine(parentNode, statements[0], currentSourceFile)
    3910            8 :             );
    3911            8 : 
    3912            8 :         let format = ListFormat.CaseOrDefaultClauseStatements;
    3913            8 :         if (emitAsSingleStatement) {
    3914            8 :             writeToken(SyntaxKind.ColonToken, colonPos, writePunctuation, parentNode);
    3915            8 :             writeSpace();
    3916            8 :             format &= ~(ListFormat.MultiLine | ListFormat.Indented);
    3917            8 :         }
    3918            8 :         else {
    3919            8 :             emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.ColonToken, colonPos, writePunctuation, parentNode);
    3920            8 :         }
    3921            8 :         emitList(parentNode, statements, format);
    3922            8 :     }

    3933            8 :         writeSpace();

    3947            8 :     function emitPropertyAssignment(node: PropertyAssignment) {
    3948            8 :         emit(node.name);
    3949            8 :         writePunctuation(":");
    3950            8 :         writeSpace();
    3951            8 :         // This is to ensure that we emit comment in the following case:
    3952            8 :         //      For example:
    3953            8 :         //          obj = {
    3954            8 :         //              id: /*comment1*/ ()=>void
    3955            8 :         //          }
    3956            8 :         // "comment1" is not considered to be leading comment for node.initializer
    3957            8 :         // but rather a trailing comment on the previous node.
    3958            8 :         const initializer = node.initializer;
    3959            8 :         if ((getEmitFlags(initializer) & EmitFlags.NoLeadingComments) === 0) {
    3960            8 :             const commentRange = getCommentRange(initializer);
    3961            8 :             emitTrailingCommentsOfPosition(commentRange.pos);
    3962            8 :         }
    3963            8 :         emitExpression(initializer, parenthesizer.parenthesizeExpressionForDisallowedComma);
    3964            8 :     }

    3971            8 :             writeSpace();
    3972            8 :             emitExpression(node.objectAssignmentInitializer, parenthesizer.parenthesizeExpressionForDisallowedComma);
    3973            8 :         }
    3974            8 :     }

    3981            8 :     }

    3995            8 :     function emitJSDoc(node: JSDoc) {

    4012            8 :                 writeSpace();

    4014            8 :             }

    4017            8 :             }
    4018            8 :         }
    4019            8 :         writeSpace();

    4181            8 :     //
    4182            8 :     // Top-level nodes
    4183            8 :     //
    4184            8 : 
    4185            8 :     function emitSourceFile(node: SourceFile) {
    4186            8 :         writeLine();
    4187            8 :         const statements = node.statements;
    4188            8 :         // Emit detached comment if there are no prologue directives or if the first node is synthesized.
    4189            8 :         // The synthesized node will have no leading comment so some comments may be missed.
    4190            8 :         const shouldEmitDetachedComment = statements.length === 0 ||
    4191            8 :             !isPrologueDirective(statements[0]) ||
    4192            8 :             nodeIsSynthesized(statements[0]);
    4193            8 :         if (shouldEmitDetachedComment) {
    4194            8 :             emitBodyWithDetachedComments(node, statements, emitSourceFileWorker);
    4195            8 :             return;
    4196            8 :         }
    4197            8 :         emitSourceFileWorker(node);
    4198            8 :     }
    4199            8 : 
    4200            8 :     function emitSyntheticTripleSlashReferencesIfNeeded(node: Bundle) {
    4201            8 :         emitTripleSlashDirectives(!!node.hasNoDefaultLib, node.syntheticFileReferences || [], node.syntheticTypeReferences || [], node.syntheticLibReferences || []);
    4202            8 :     }
    4203            8 : 
    4204            8 :     function emitTripleSlashDirectivesIfNeeded(node: SourceFile) {
    4205            8 :         if (node.isDeclarationFile) emitTripleSlashDirectives(node.hasNoDefaultLib, node.referencedFiles, node.typeReferenceDirectives, node.libReferenceDirectives);
    4206            8 :     }
    4207            8 : 
    4208            8 :     function emitTripleSlashDirectives(hasNoDefaultLib: boolean, files: readonly FileReference[], types: readonly FileReference[], libs: readonly FileReference[]) {
    4209            8 :         if (hasNoDefaultLib) {
    4210            8 :             writeComment(`/// <reference no-default-lib="true"/>`);
    4211            8 :             writeLine();
    4212            8 :         }
    4213            8 :         if (currentSourceFile && currentSourceFile.moduleName) {
    4214            8 :             writeComment(`/// <amd-module name="${currentSourceFile.moduleName}" />`);
    4215            8 :             writeLine();
    4216            8 :         }
    4217            8 :         if (currentSourceFile && currentSourceFile.amdDependencies) {
    4218            8 :             for (const dep of currentSourceFile.amdDependencies) {
    4219            8 :                 if (dep.name) {
    4220            8 :                     writeComment(`/// <amd-dependency name="${dep.name}" path="${dep.path}" />`);
    4221            8 :                 }
    4222            8 :                 else {
    4223            8 :                     writeComment(`/// <amd-dependency path="${dep.path}" />`);
    4224            8 :                 }
    4225            8 :                 writeLine();
    4226            8 :             }
    4227            8 :         }
    4228            8 : 
    4229            8 :         function writeDirectives(kind: "path" | "types" | "lib", directives: readonly FileReference[]) {
    4230            8 :             for (const directive of directives) {
    4231            8 :                 const resolutionMode = directive.resolutionMode
    4232            8 :                     ? `resolution-mode="${directive.resolutionMode === ModuleKind.ESNext ? "import" : "require"}" `
    4233            8 :                     : "";
    4234            8 :                 const preserve = directive.preserve ? `preserve="true" ` : "";
    4235            8 :                 writeComment(`/// <reference ${kind}="${directive.fileName}" ${resolutionMode}${preserve}/>`);
    4236            8 :                 writeLine();
    4237            8 :             }
    4238            8 :         }
    4239            8 : 
    4240            8 :         writeDirectives("path", files);
    4241            8 :         writeDirectives("types", types);
    4242            8 :         writeDirectives("lib", libs);
    4243            8 :     }
    4244            8 : 
    4245            8 :     function emitSourceFileWorker(node: SourceFile) {
    4246            8 :         const statements = node.statements;
    4247            8 :         pushNameGenerationScope(node);
    4248            8 :         forEach(node.statements, generateNames);
    4249            8 :         emitHelpers(node);
    4250            8 :         const index = findIndex(statements, statement => !isPrologueDirective(statement));
    4251            8 :         emitTripleSlashDirectivesIfNeeded(node);
    4252            8 :         emitList(node, statements, ListFormat.MultiLine, /*parenthesizerRule*/ undefined, index === -1 ? statements.length : index);
    4253            8 :         popNameGenerationScope(node);
    4254            8 :     }
    4255            8 : 
    4256            8 :     // Transformation nodes
    4257            8 : 
    4258            8 :     function emitPartiallyEmittedExpression(node: PartiallyEmittedExpression) {
    4259            8 :         const emitFlags = getEmitFlags(node);
    4260            8 :         if (!(emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoLeadingComments) && node.pos !== node.expression.pos) {
    4261            8 :             emitTrailingCommentsOfPosition(node.expression.pos);
    4262            8 :         }
    4263            8 :         emitExpression(node.expression);
    4264            8 :         if (!(emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingComments) && node.end !== node.expression.end) {
    4265            8 :             emitLeadingCommentsOfPosition(node.expression.end);
    4266            8 :         }
    4267            8 :     }
    4268            8 : 
    4269            8 :     function emitCommaList(node: CommaListExpression) {

    4273            8 :     /**
    4274            8 :      * Emits any prologue directives at the start of a Statement list, returning the
    4275            8 :      * number of prologue directives written to the output.
    4276            8 :      */
    4277            8 :     function emitPrologueDirectives(statements: readonly Node[], sourceFile?: SourceFile, seenPrologueDirectives?: Set<string>): number {
    4278            8 :         let needsToSetSourceFile = !!sourceFile;
    4279            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < statements.length; i++) {
    4280            8 :             const statement = statements[i];
    4281            8 :             if (isPrologueDirective(statement)) {
    4282            8 :                 const shouldEmitPrologueDirective = seenPrologueDirectives ? !seenPrologueDirectives.has(statement.expression.text) : true;
    4283            8 :                 if (shouldEmitPrologueDirective) {
    4284            8 :                     if (needsToSetSourceFile) {
    4285            8 :                         needsToSetSourceFile = false;
    4286            8 :                         setSourceFile(sourceFile);
    4287            8 :                     }
    4288            8 :                     writeLine();
    4289            8 :                     emit(statement);
    4290            8 :                     if (seenPrologueDirectives) {
    4291            8 :                         seenPrologueDirectives.add(statement.expression.text);
    4292            8 :                     }
    4293            8 :                 }
    4294            8 :             }
    4295            8 :             else {
    4296            8 :                 // return index of the first non prologue directive
    4297            8 :                 return i;
    4298            8 :             }
    4299            8 :         }
    4300            8 : 
    4301            8 :         return statements.length;
    4302            8 :     }
    4303            8 : 
    4304            8 :     function emitPrologueDirectivesIfNeeded(sourceFileOrBundle: Bundle | SourceFile) {
    4305            8 :         if (isSourceFile(sourceFileOrBundle)) {
    4306            8 :             emitPrologueDirectives(sourceFileOrBundle.statements, sourceFileOrBundle);
    4307            8 :         }
    4308            8 :         else {
    4309            8 :             const seenPrologueDirectives = new Set<string>();
    4310            8 :             for (const sourceFile of sourceFileOrBundle.sourceFiles) {
    4311            8 :                 emitPrologueDirectives(sourceFile.statements, sourceFile, seenPrologueDirectives);
    4312            8 :             }
    4313            8 :             setSourceFile(undefined);
    4314            8 :         }
    4315            8 :     }

    4317            8 :     function emitShebangIfNeeded(sourceFileOrBundle: Bundle | SourceFile) {
    4318            8 :         if (isSourceFile(sourceFileOrBundle)) {
    4319            8 :             const shebang = getShebang(sourceFileOrBundle.text);
    4320            8 :             if (shebang) {
    4321            8 :                 writeComment(shebang);
    4322            8 :                 writeLine();
    4323            8 :                 return true;
    4324            8 :             }
    4325            8 :         }
    4326            8 :         else {
    4327            8 :             for (const sourceFile of sourceFileOrBundle.sourceFiles) {
    4328            8 :                 // Emit only the first encountered shebang
    4329            8 :                 if (emitShebangIfNeeded(sourceFile)) {
    4330            8 :                     return true;
    4331            8 :                 }
    4332            8 :             }
    4333            8 :         }
    4334            8 :     }

    4340            8 :     function emitNodeWithWriter(node: Node | undefined, writer: typeof write) {
    4341            8 :         if (!node) return;
    4342            8 :         const savedWrite = write;
    4343            8 :         write = writer;

    4348            8 :     function emitDecoratorsAndModifiers(node: Node, modifiers: NodeArray<ModifierLike> | undefined, allowDecorators: boolean) {
    4349            8 :         if (modifiers?.length) {
    4350            8 :             if (every(modifiers, isModifier)) {
    4351            8 :                 // if all modifier-likes are `Modifier`, simply emit the array as modifiers.
    4352            8 :                 return emitModifierList(node, modifiers as NodeArray<Modifier>);
    4353            8 :             }
    4354            8 : 
    4355            8 :             if (every(modifiers, isDecorator)) {
    4356            8 :                 if (allowDecorators) {
    4357            8 :                     // if all modifier-likes are `Decorator`, simply emit the array as decorators.
    4358            8 :                     return emitDecoratorList(node, modifiers as NodeArray<Decorator>);
    4359            8 :                 }
    4360            8 :                 return node.pos;
    4361            8 :             }
    4362            8 : 
    4363            8 :             onBeforeEmitNodeArray?.(modifiers);
    4364            8 : 
    4365            8 :             // partition modifiers into contiguous chunks of `Modifier` or `Decorator`
    4366            8 :             let lastMode: "modifiers" | "decorators" | undefined;
    4367            8 :             let mode: "modifiers" | "decorators" | undefined;
    4368            8 :             let start = 0;
    4369            8 :             let pos = 0;
    4370            8 :             let lastModifier: ModifierLike | undefined;
    4371            8 :             while (start < modifiers.length) {
    4372            8 :                 while (pos < modifiers.length) {
    4373            8 :                     lastModifier = modifiers[pos];
    4374            8 :                     mode = isDecorator(lastModifier) ? "decorators" : "modifiers";
    4375            8 :                     if (lastMode === undefined) {
    4376            8 :                         lastMode = mode;
    4377            8 :                     }
    4378            8 :                     else if (mode !== lastMode) {
    4379            8 :                         break;
    4380            8 :                     }
    4381            8 : 
    4382            8 :                     pos++;
    4383            8 :                 }
    4384            8 : 
    4385            8 :                 const textRange: TextRange = { pos: -1, end: -1 };
    4386            8 :                 if (start === 0) textRange.pos = modifiers.pos;
    4387            8 :                 if (pos === modifiers.length - 1) textRange.end = modifiers.end;
    4388            8 :                 if (lastMode === "modifiers" || allowDecorators) {
    4389            8 :                     emitNodeListItems(
    4390            8 :                         emit,
    4391            8 :                         node,
    4392            8 :                         modifiers,
    4393            8 :                         lastMode === "modifiers" ? ListFormat.Modifiers : ListFormat.Decorators,
    4394            8 :                         /*parenthesizerRule*/ undefined,
    4395            8 :                         start,
    4396            8 :                         pos - start,
    4397            8 :                         /*hasTrailingComma*/ false,
    4398            8 :                         textRange,
    4399            8 :                     );
    4400            8 :                 }
    4401            8 :                 start = pos;
    4402            8 :                 lastMode = mode;
    4403            8 :                 pos++;
    4404            8 :             }
    4405            8 : 
    4406            8 :             onAfterEmitNodeArray?.(modifiers);
    4407            8 : 
    4408            8 :             if (lastModifier && !positionIsSynthesized(lastModifier.end)) {
    4409            8 :                 return lastModifier.end;
    4410            8 :             }
    4411            8 :         }
    4412            8 : 
    4413            8 :         return node.pos;
    4414            8 :     }

    4510            8 :     function canEmitSimpleArrowHead(parentNode: FunctionTypeNode | ConstructorTypeNode | ArrowFunction, parameters: NodeArray<ParameterDeclaration>) {
    4511            8 :         const parameter = singleOrUndefined(parameters);
    4512            8 :         return parameter
    4513            8 :             && parameter.pos === parentNode.pos // may not have parsed tokens between parent and parameter
    4514            8 :             && isArrowFunction(parentNode) // only arrow functions may have simple arrow head
    4515            8 :             && !parentNode.type // arrow function may not have return type annotation
    4516            8 :             && !some(parentNode.modifiers) // parent may not have decorators or modifiers
    4517            8 :             && !some(parentNode.typeParameters) // parent may not have type parameters
    4518            8 :             && !some(parameter.modifiers) // parameter may not have decorators or modifiers
    4519            8 :             && !parameter.dotDotDotToken // parameter may not be rest
    4520            8 :             && !parameter.questionToken // parameter may not be optional
    4521            8 :             && !parameter.type // parameter may not have a type annotation
    4522            8 :             && !parameter.initializer // parameter may not have an initializer
    4523            8 :             && isIdentifier(parameter.name); // parameter name must be identifier
    4524            8 :     }

    4539            8 :     function writeDelimiter(format: ListFormat) {
    4540            8 :         switch (format & ListFormat.DelimitersMask) {
    4541            8 :             case ListFormat.None:
    4542            8 :                 break;

    4544            8 :                 writePunctuation(",");
    4545            8 :                 break;
    4546            8 :             case ListFormat.BarDelimited:
    4547            8 :                 writeSpace();
    4548            8 :                 writePunctuation("|");
    4549            8 :                 break;
    4550            8 :             case ListFormat.AsteriskDelimited:
    4551            8 :                 writeSpace();
    4552            8 :                 writePunctuation("*");
    4553            8 :                 writeSpace();
    4554            8 :                 break;
    4555            8 :             case ListFormat.AmpersandDelimited:
    4556            8 :                 writeSpace();
    4557            8 :                 writePunctuation("&");

    4559            8 :         }
    4560            8 :     }

    4578            8 :     function emitNodeList<Child extends Node, Children extends NodeArray<Child>>(emit: EmitFunction, parentNode: Node | undefined, children: Children | undefined, format: ListFormat, parenthesizerRule: ParenthesizerRuleOrSelector<Child> | undefined, start = 0, count = children ? children.length - start : 0) {
    4579            8 :         const isUndefined = children === undefined;
    4580            8 :         if (isUndefined && format & ListFormat.OptionalIfUndefined) {
    4581            8 :             return;

    4585            8 :         if (isEmpty && format & ListFormat.OptionalIfEmpty) {
    4586            8 :             onBeforeEmitNodeArray?.(children);
    4587            8 :             onAfterEmitNodeArray?.(children);

    4622            8 : 
    4623            8 :     /**
    4624            8 :      * Emits a list without brackets or raising events.
    4625            8 :      *
    4626            8 :      * NOTE: You probably don't want to call this directly and should be using `emitList` or `emitExpressionList` instead.
    4627            8 :      */
    4628            8 :     function emitNodeListItems<Child extends Node>(emit: EmitFunction, parentNode: Node | undefined, children: readonly Child[], format: ListFormat, parenthesizerRule: ParenthesizerRuleOrSelector<Child> | undefined, start: number, count: number, hasTrailingComma: boolean, childrenTextRange: TextRange | undefined) {
    4629            8 :         // Write the opening line terminator or leading whitespace.
    4630            8 :         const mayEmitInterveningComments = (format & ListFormat.NoInterveningComments) === 0;
    4631            8 :         let shouldEmitInterveningComments = mayEmitInterveningComments;
    4632            8 : 
    4633            8 :         const leadingLineTerminatorCount = getLeadingLineTerminatorCount(parentNode, children[start], format);
    4634            8 :         if (leadingLineTerminatorCount) {
    4635            8 :             writeLine(leadingLineTerminatorCount);
    4636            8 :             shouldEmitInterveningComments = false;
    4637            8 :         }
    4638            8 :         else if (format & ListFormat.SpaceBetweenBraces) {
    4639            8 :             writeSpace();
    4640            8 :         }
    4641            8 : 
    4642            8 :         // Increase the indent, if requested.
    4643            8 :         if (format & ListFormat.Indented) {
    4644            8 :             increaseIndent();
    4645            8 :         }
    4646            8 : 
    4647            8 :         const emitListItem = getEmitListItem(emit, parenthesizerRule);
    4648            8 : 
    4649            8 :         // Emit each child.
    4650            8 :         let previousSibling: Node | undefined;
    4651            8 :         let shouldDecreaseIndentAfterEmit = false;
    4652            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    4653            8 :             const child = children[start + i];
    4654            8 : 
    4655            8 :             // Write the delimiter if this is not the first node.
    4656            8 :             if (format & ListFormat.AsteriskDelimited) {
    4657            8 :                 // always write JSDoc in the format "\n *"
    4658            8 :                 writeLine();
    4659            8 :                 writeDelimiter(format);
    4660            8 :             }
    4661            8 :             else if (previousSibling) {
    4662            8 :                 // i.e
    4663            8 :                 //      function commentedParameters(
    4664            8 :                 //          /* Parameter a */
    4665            8 :                 //          a
    4666            8 :                 //          /* End of parameter a */ -> this comment isn't considered to be trailing comment of parameter "a" due to newline
    4667            8 :                 //          ,
    4668            8 :                 if (format & ListFormat.DelimitersMask && previousSibling.end !== (parentNode ? parentNode.end : -1)) {
    4669            8 :                     const previousSiblingEmitFlags = getEmitFlags(previousSibling);
    4670            8 :                     if (!(previousSiblingEmitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingComments)) {
    4671            8 :                         emitLeadingCommentsOfPosition(previousSibling.end);
    4672            8 :                     }
    4673            8 :                 }
    4674            8 : 
    4675            8 :                 writeDelimiter(format);
    4676            8 : 
    4677            8 :                 // Write either a line terminator or whitespace to separate the elements.
    4678            8 :                 const separatingLineTerminatorCount = getSeparatingLineTerminatorCount(previousSibling, child, format);
    4679            8 :                 if (separatingLineTerminatorCount > 0) {
    4680            8 :                     // If a synthesized node in a single-line list starts on a new
    4681            8 :                     // line, we should increase the indent.
    4682            8 :                     if ((format & (ListFormat.LinesMask | ListFormat.Indented)) === ListFormat.SingleLine) {
    4683            8 :                         increaseIndent();
    4684            8 :                         shouldDecreaseIndentAfterEmit = true;
    4685            8 :                     }
    4686            8 : 
    4687            8 :                     if (shouldEmitInterveningComments && format & ListFormat.DelimitersMask && !positionIsSynthesized(child.pos)) {
    4688            8 :                         const commentRange = getCommentRange(child);
    4689            8 :                         emitTrailingCommentsOfPosition(commentRange.pos, /*prefixSpace*/ !!(format & ListFormat.SpaceBetweenSiblings), /*forceNoNewline*/ true);
    4690            8 :                     }
    4691            8 : 
    4692            8 :                     writeLine(separatingLineTerminatorCount);
    4693            8 :                     shouldEmitInterveningComments = false;
    4694            8 :                 }
    4695            8 :                 else if (previousSibling && format & ListFormat.SpaceBetweenSiblings) {
    4696            8 :                     writeSpace();
    4697            8 :                 }
    4698            8 :             }
    4699            8 : 
    4700            8 :             // Emit this child.
    4701            8 :             if (shouldEmitInterveningComments) {
    4702            8 :                 const commentRange = getCommentRange(child);
    4703            8 :                 emitTrailingCommentsOfPosition(commentRange.pos);
    4704            8 :             }
    4705            8 :             else {
    4706            8 :                 shouldEmitInterveningComments = mayEmitInterveningComments;
    4707            8 :             }
    4708            8 : 
    4709            8 :             nextListElementPos = child.pos;
    4710            8 :             emitListItem(child, emit, parenthesizerRule, i);
    4711            8 : 
    4712            8 :             if (shouldDecreaseIndentAfterEmit) {
    4713            8 :                 decreaseIndent();
    4714            8 :                 shouldDecreaseIndentAfterEmit = false;
    4715            8 :             }
    4716            8 : 
    4717            8 :             previousSibling = child;
    4718            8 :         }
    4719            8 : 
    4720            8 :         // Write a trailing comma, if requested.
    4721            8 :         const emitFlags = previousSibling ? getEmitFlags(previousSibling) : 0;
    4722            8 :         const skipTrailingComments = commentsDisabled || !!(emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingComments);
    4723            8 :         const emitTrailingComma = hasTrailingComma && (format & ListFormat.AllowTrailingComma) && (format & ListFormat.CommaDelimited);
    4724            8 :         if (emitTrailingComma) {
    4725            8 :             if (previousSibling && !skipTrailingComments) {
    4726            8 :                 emitTokenWithComment(SyntaxKind.CommaToken, previousSibling.end, writePunctuation, previousSibling);
    4727            8 :             }
    4728            8 :             else {
    4729            8 :                 writePunctuation(",");
    4730            8 :             }
    4731            8 :         }
    4732            8 : 
    4733            8 :         // Emit any trailing comment of the last element in the list
    4734            8 :         // i.e
    4735            8 :         //       var array = [...
    4736            8 :         //          2
    4737            8 :         //          /* end of element 2 */
    4738            8 :         //       ];
    4739            8 :         if (previousSibling && (parentNode ? parentNode.end : -1) !== previousSibling.end && (format & ListFormat.DelimitersMask) && !skipTrailingComments) {
    4740            8 :             emitLeadingCommentsOfPosition(emitTrailingComma && childrenTextRange?.end ? childrenTextRange.end : previousSibling.end);
    4741            8 :         }
    4742            8 : 
    4743            8 :         // Decrease the indent, if requested.
    4744            8 :         if (format & ListFormat.Indented) {
    4745            8 :             decreaseIndent();
    4746            8 :         }
    4747            8 : 
    4748            8 :         // Write the closing line terminator or closing whitespace.
    4749            8 :         const closingLineTerminatorCount = getClosingLineTerminatorCount(parentNode, children[start + count - 1], format, childrenTextRange);
    4750            8 :         if (closingLineTerminatorCount) {
    4751            8 :             writeLine(closingLineTerminatorCount);
    4752            8 :         }
    4753            8 :         else if (format & (ListFormat.SpaceAfterList | ListFormat.SpaceBetweenBraces)) {
    4754            8 :             writeSpace();
    4755            8 :         }
    4756            8 :     }
    4757            8 :

    4832            8 :     function writeToken(token: SyntaxKind, pos: number, writer: (s: string) => void, contextNode?: Node) {

    4834            8 :             ? emitTokenWithSourceMap(contextNode, token, writer, pos, writeTokenText)
    4835            8 :             : writeTokenText(token, writer, pos);

    4850            8 :     function writeTokenText(token: SyntaxKind, writer: (s: string) => void, pos?: number): number {
    4851            8 :         const tokenString = tokenToString(token)!;
    4852            8 :         writer(tokenString);
    4853            8 :         return pos! < 0 ? pos! : pos! + tokenString.length;
    4854            8 :     }
    4855            8 : 
    4856            8 :     function writeLineOrSpace(parentNode: Node, prevChildNode: Node, nextChildNode: Node) {
    4857            8 :         if (getEmitFlags(parentNode) & EmitFlags.SingleLine) {
    4858            8 :             writeSpace();
    4859            8 :         }
    4860            8 :         else if (preserveSourceNewlines) {
    4861            8 :             const lines = getLinesBetweenNodes(parentNode, prevChildNode, nextChildNode);
    4862            8 :             if (lines) {
    4863            8 :                 writeLine(lines);
    4864            8 :             }
    4865            8 :             else {
    4866            8 :                 writeSpace();
    4867            8 :             }
    4868            8 :         }
    4869            8 :         else {
    4870            8 :             writeLine();
    4871            8 :         }
    4872            8 :     }
    4873            8 : 
    4874            8 :     function writeLines(text: string): void {
    4875            8 :         const lines = text.split(/\r\n?|\n/g);
    4876            8 :         const indentation = guessIndentation(lines);
    4877            8 :         for (const lineText of lines) {
    4878            8 :             const line = indentation ? lineText.slice(indentation) : lineText;
    4879            8 :             if (line.length) {
    4880            8 :                 writeLine();
    4881            8 :                 write(line);
    4882            8 :             }
    4883            8 :         }
    4884            8 :     }
    4885            8 : 
    4886            8 :     function writeLinesAndIndent(lineCount: number, writeSpaceIfNotIndenting: boolean) {
    4887            8 :         if (lineCount) {
    4888            8 :             increaseIndent();
    4889            8 :             writeLine(lineCount);
    4890            8 :         }
    4891            8 :         else if (writeSpaceIfNotIndenting) {
    4892            8 :             writeSpace();
    4893            8 :         }
    4894            8 :     }
    4895            8 : 
    4896            8 :     // Helper function to decrease the indent if we previously indented.  Allows multiple
    4897            8 :     // previous indent values to be considered at a time.  This also allows caller to just
    4898            8 :     // call this once, passing in all their appropriate indent values, instead of needing
    4899            8 :     // to call this helper function multiple times.
    4900            8 :     function decreaseIndentIf(value1: boolean | number | undefined, value2?: boolean | number) {
    4901            8 :         if (value1) {
    4902            8 :             decreaseIndent();
    4903            8 :         }
    4904            8 :         if (value2) {
    4905            8 :             decreaseIndent();
    4906            8 :         }
    4907            8 :     }
    4908            8 : 
    4909            8 :     function getLeadingLineTerminatorCount(parentNode: Node | undefined, firstChild: Node | undefined, format: ListFormat): number {
    4910            8 :         if (format & ListFormat.PreserveLines || preserveSourceNewlines) {
    4911            8 :             if (format & ListFormat.PreferNewLine) {
    4912            8 :                 return 1;
    4913            8 :             }
    4914            8 : 
    4915            8 :             if (firstChild === undefined) {
    4916            8 :                 return !parentNode || currentSourceFile && rangeIsOnSingleLine(parentNode, currentSourceFile) ? 0 : 1;
    4917            8 :             }
    4918            8 :             if (firstChild.pos === nextListElementPos) {
    4919            8 :                 // If this child starts at the beginning of a list item in a parent list, its leading
    4920            8 :                 // line terminators have already been written as the separating line terminators of the
    4921            8 :                 // parent list. Example:
    4922            8 :                 //
    4923            8 :                 // class Foo {
    4924            8 :                 //   constructor() {}
    4925            8 :                 //   public foo() {}
    4926            8 :                 // }
    4927            8 :                 //
    4928            8 :                 // The outer list is the list of class members, with one line terminator between the
    4929            8 :                 // constructor and the method. The constructor is written, the separating line terminator
    4930            8 :                 // is written, and then we start emitting the method. Its modifiers ([public]) constitute an inner
    4931            8 :                 // list, so we look for its leading line terminators. If we didn't know that we had already
    4932            8 :                 // written a newline as part of the parent list, it would appear that we need to write a
    4933            8 :                 // leading newline to start the modifiers.
    4934            8 :                 return 0;
    4935            8 :             }
    4936            8 :             if (firstChild.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxText) {
    4937            8 :                 // JsxText will be written with its leading whitespace, so don't add more manually.
    4938            8 :                 return 0;
    4939            8 :             }
    4940            8 :             if (
    4941            8 :                 currentSourceFile && parentNode &&
    4942            8 :                 !positionIsSynthesized(parentNode.pos) &&
    4943            8 :                 !nodeIsSynthesized(firstChild) &&
    4944            8 :                 (!firstChild.parent || getOriginalNode(firstChild.parent) === getOriginalNode(parentNode))
    4945            8 :             ) {
    4946            8 :                 if (preserveSourceNewlines) {
    4947            8 :                     return getEffectiveLines(
    4948            8 :                         includeComments =>
    4949            8 :                             getLinesBetweenPositionAndPrecedingNonWhitespaceCharacter(
    4950            8 :                                 firstChild.pos,
    4951            8 :                                 parentNode.pos,
    4952            8 :                                 currentSourceFile!,
    4953            8 :                                 includeComments,
    4954            8 :                             ),
    4955            8 :                     );
    4956            8 :                 }
    4957            8 :                 return rangeStartPositionsAreOnSameLine(parentNode, firstChild, currentSourceFile) ? 0 : 1;
    4958            8 :             }
    4959            8 :             if (synthesizedNodeStartsOnNewLine(firstChild, format)) {
    4960            8 :                 return 1;
    4961            8 :             }
    4962            8 :         }
    4963            8 :         return format & ListFormat.MultiLine ? 1 : 0;
    4964            8 :     }
    4965            8 : 
    4966            8 :     function getSeparatingLineTerminatorCount(previousNode: Node | undefined, nextNode: Node, format: ListFormat): number {
    4967            8 :         if (format & ListFormat.PreserveLines || preserveSourceNewlines) {
    4968            8 :             if (previousNode === undefined || nextNode === undefined) {
    4969            8 :                 return 0;
    4970            8 :             }
    4971            8 :             if (nextNode.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxText) {
    4972            8 :                 // JsxText will be written with its leading whitespace, so don't add more manually.
    4973            8 :                 return 0;
    4974            8 :             }
    4975            8 :             else if (currentSourceFile && !nodeIsSynthesized(previousNode) && !nodeIsSynthesized(nextNode)) {
    4976            8 :                 if (preserveSourceNewlines && siblingNodePositionsAreComparable(previousNode, nextNode)) {
    4977            8 :                     return getEffectiveLines(
    4978            8 :                         includeComments =>
    4979            8 :                             getLinesBetweenRangeEndAndRangeStart(
    4980            8 :                                 previousNode,
    4981            8 :                                 nextNode,
    4982            8 :                                 currentSourceFile!,
    4983            8 :                                 includeComments,
    4984            8 :                             ),
    4985            8 :                     );
    4986            8 :                 }
    4987            8 :                 // If `preserveSourceNewlines` is `false` we do not intend to preserve the effective lines between the
    4988            8 :                 // previous and next node. Instead we naively check whether nodes are on separate lines within the
    4989            8 :                 // same node parent. If so, we intend to preserve a single line terminator. This is less precise and
    4990            8 :                 // expensive than checking with `preserveSourceNewlines` as above, but the goal is not to preserve the
    4991            8 :                 // effective source lines between two sibling nodes.
    4992            8 :                 else if (!preserveSourceNewlines && originalNodesHaveSameParent(previousNode, nextNode)) {
    4993            8 :                     return rangeEndIsOnSameLineAsRangeStart(previousNode, nextNode, currentSourceFile) ? 0 : 1;
    4994            8 :                 }
    4995            8 :                 // If the two nodes are not comparable, add a line terminator based on the format that can indicate
    4996            8 :                 // whether new lines are preferred or not.
    4997            8 :                 return format & ListFormat.PreferNewLine ? 1 : 0;
    4998            8 :             }
    4999            8 :             else if (synthesizedNodeStartsOnNewLine(previousNode, format) || synthesizedNodeStartsOnNewLine(nextNode, format)) {
    5000            8 :                 return 1;
    5001            8 :             }
    5002            8 :         }
    5003            8 :         else if (getStartsOnNewLine(nextNode)) {
    5004            8 :             return 1;
    5005            8 :         }
