    5006            8 :         return format & ListFormat.MultiLine ? 1 : 0;
    5007            8 :     }
    5008            8 : 
    5009            8 :     function getClosingLineTerminatorCount(parentNode: Node | undefined, lastChild: Node | undefined, format: ListFormat, childrenTextRange: TextRange | undefined): number {
    5010            8 :         if (format & ListFormat.PreserveLines || preserveSourceNewlines) {
    5011            8 :             if (format & ListFormat.PreferNewLine) {
    5012            8 :                 return 1;
    5013            8 :             }
    5014            8 : 
    5015            8 :             if (lastChild === undefined) {
    5016            8 :                 return !parentNode || currentSourceFile && rangeIsOnSingleLine(parentNode, currentSourceFile) ? 0 : 1;
    5017            8 :             }
    5018            8 :             if (currentSourceFile && parentNode && !positionIsSynthesized(parentNode.pos) && !nodeIsSynthesized(lastChild) && (!lastChild.parent || lastChild.parent === parentNode)) {
    5019            8 :                 if (preserveSourceNewlines) {
    5020            8 :                     const end = childrenTextRange && !positionIsSynthesized(childrenTextRange.end) ? childrenTextRange.end : lastChild.end;
    5021            8 :                     return getEffectiveLines(
    5022            8 :                         includeComments =>
    5023            8 :                             getLinesBetweenPositionAndNextNonWhitespaceCharacter(
    5024            8 :                                 end,
    5025            8 :                                 parentNode.end,
    5026            8 :                                 currentSourceFile!,
    5027            8 :                                 includeComments,
    5028            8 :                             ),
    5029            8 :                     );
    5030            8 :                 }
    5031            8 :                 return rangeEndPositionsAreOnSameLine(parentNode, lastChild, currentSourceFile) ? 0 : 1;
    5032            8 :             }
    5033            8 :             if (synthesizedNodeStartsOnNewLine(lastChild, format)) {
    5034            8 :                 return 1;
    5035            8 :             }
    5036            8 :         }
    5037            8 :         if (format & ListFormat.MultiLine && !(format & ListFormat.NoTrailingNewLine)) {
    5038            8 :             return 1;
    5039            8 :         }
    5040            8 :         return 0;
    5041            8 :     }
    5042            8 : 
    5043            8 :     function getEffectiveLines(getLineDifference: (includeComments: boolean) => number) {
    5044            8 :         // If 'preserveSourceNewlines' is disabled, we should never call this function
    5045            8 :         // because it could be more expensive than alternative approximations.
    5046            8 :         Debug.assert(!!preserveSourceNewlines);
    5047            8 :         // We start by measuring the line difference from a position to its adjacent comments,
    5048            8 :         // so that this is counted as a one-line difference, not two:
    5049            8 :         //
    5050            8 :         //   node1;
    5051            8 :         //   // NODE2 COMMENT
    5052            8 :         //   node2;
    5053            8 :         const lines = getLineDifference(/*includeComments*/ true);
    5054            8 :         if (lines === 0) {
    5055            8 :             // However, if the line difference considering comments was 0, we might have this:
    5056            8 :             //
    5057            8 :             //   node1; // NODE2 COMMENT
    5058            8 :             //   node2;
    5059            8 :             //
    5060            8 :             // in which case we should be ignoring node2's comment, so this too is counted as
    5061            8 :             // a one-line difference, not zero.
    5062            8 :             return getLineDifference(/*includeComments*/ false);
    5063            8 :         }
    5064            8 :         return lines;
    5065            8 :     }
    5066            8 : 
    5067            8 :     function writeLineSeparatorsAndIndentBefore(node: Node, parent: Node): boolean {
    5068            8 :         const leadingNewlines = preserveSourceNewlines && getLeadingLineTerminatorCount(parent, node, ListFormat.None);
    5069            8 :         if (leadingNewlines) {
    5070            8 :             writeLinesAndIndent(leadingNewlines, /*writeSpaceIfNotIndenting*/ false);
    5071            8 :         }
    5072            8 :         return !!leadingNewlines;
    5073            8 :     }
    5074            8 : 
    5075            8 :     function writeLineSeparatorsAfter(node: Node, parent: Node) {
    5076            8 :         const trailingNewlines = preserveSourceNewlines && getClosingLineTerminatorCount(parent, node, ListFormat.None, /*childrenTextRange*/ undefined);
    5077            8 :         if (trailingNewlines) {
    5078            8 :             writeLine(trailingNewlines);
    5079            8 :         }
    5080            8 :     }
    5081            8 : 
    5082            8 :     function synthesizedNodeStartsOnNewLine(node: Node, format: ListFormat) {
    5083            8 :         if (nodeIsSynthesized(node)) {
    5084            8 :             const startsOnNewLine = getStartsOnNewLine(node);
    5085            8 :             if (startsOnNewLine === undefined) {
    5086            8 :                 return (format & ListFormat.PreferNewLine) !== 0;
    5087            8 :             }
    5088            8 : 
    5089            8 :             return startsOnNewLine;
    5090            8 :         }
    5091            8 : 
    5092            8 :         return (format & ListFormat.PreferNewLine) !== 0;
    5093            8 :     }
    5094            8 : 
    5095            8 :     function getLinesBetweenNodes(parent: Node, node1: Node, node2: Node): number {
    5096            8 :         if (getEmitFlags(parent) & EmitFlags.NoIndentation) {
    5097            8 :             return 0;
    5098            8 :         }
    5099            8 : 
    5100            8 :         parent = skipSynthesizedParentheses(parent);
    5101            8 :         node1 = skipSynthesizedParentheses(node1);
    5102            8 :         node2 = skipSynthesizedParentheses(node2);
    5103            8 : 
    5104            8 :         // Always use a newline for synthesized code if the synthesizer desires it.
    5105            8 :         if (getStartsOnNewLine(node2)) {
    5106            8 :             return 1;
    5107            8 :         }
    5108            8 : 
    5109            8 :         if (currentSourceFile && !nodeIsSynthesized(parent) && !nodeIsSynthesized(node1) && !nodeIsSynthesized(node2)) {
    5110            8 :             if (preserveSourceNewlines) {
    5111            8 :                 return getEffectiveLines(
    5112            8 :                     includeComments =>
    5113            8 :                         getLinesBetweenRangeEndAndRangeStart(
    5114            8 :                             node1,
    5115            8 :                             node2,
    5116            8 :                             currentSourceFile!,
    5117            8 :                             includeComments,
    5118            8 :                         ),
    5119            8 :                 );
    5120            8 :             }
    5121            8 :             return rangeEndIsOnSameLineAsRangeStart(node1, node2, currentSourceFile) ? 0 : 1;
    5122            8 :         }
    5123            8 : 
    5124            8 :         return 0;
    5125            8 :     }
    5126            8 : 
    5127            8 :     function isEmptyBlock(block: BlockLike) {
    5128            8 :         return block.statements.length === 0
    5129            8 :             && (!currentSourceFile || rangeEndIsOnSameLineAsRangeStart(block, block, currentSourceFile));
    5130            8 :     }
    5131            8 : 
    5132            8 :     function skipSynthesizedParentheses(node: Node) {
    5133            8 :         while (node.kind === SyntaxKind.ParenthesizedExpression && nodeIsSynthesized(node)) {
    5134            8 :             node = (node as ParenthesizedExpression).expression;
    5135            8 :         }
    5136            8 : 
    5137            8 :         return node;
    5138            8 :     }
    5139            8 : 
    5140            8 :     function getTextOfNode(node: Identifier | PrivateIdentifier | LiteralExpression | JsxNamespacedName, includeTrivia?: boolean): string {
    5141            8 :         if (isGeneratedIdentifier(node) || isGeneratedPrivateIdentifier(node)) {
    5142            8 :             return generateName(node);
    5143            8 :         }
    5144            8 :         if (isStringLiteral(node) && node.textSourceNode) {
    5145            8 :             return getTextOfNode(node.textSourceNode, includeTrivia);
    5146            8 :         }
    5147            8 :         const sourceFile = currentSourceFile; // const needed for control flow
    5148            8 :         const canUseSourceFile = !!sourceFile && !!node.parent && !nodeIsSynthesized(node);
    5149            8 :         if (isMemberName(node)) {
    5150            8 :             if (!canUseSourceFile || getSourceFileOfNode(node) !== getOriginalNode(sourceFile)) {
    5151            8 :                 return idText(node);
    5152            8 :             }
    5153            8 :         }
    5154            8 :         else if (isJsxNamespacedName(node)) {
    5155            8 :             if (!canUseSourceFile || getSourceFileOfNode(node) !== getOriginalNode(sourceFile)) {
    5156            8 :                 return getTextOfJsxNamespacedName(node);
    5157            8 :             }
    5158            8 :         }
    5159            8 :         else {
    5160            8 :             Debug.assertNode(node, isLiteralExpression); // not strictly necessary
    5161            8 :             if (!canUseSourceFile) {
    5162            8 :                 return node.text;
    5163            8 :             }
    5164            8 :         }
    5165            8 :         return getSourceTextOfNodeFromSourceFile(sourceFile, node, includeTrivia);
    5166            8 :     }
    5167            8 : 
    5168            8 :     function getLiteralTextOfNode(node: LiteralLikeNode, neverAsciiEscape: boolean | undefined, jsxAttributeEscape: boolean): string {
    5169            8 :         if (node.kind === SyntaxKind.StringLiteral && (node as StringLiteral).textSourceNode) {
    5170            8 :             const textSourceNode = (node as StringLiteral).textSourceNode!;
    5171            8 :             if (isIdentifier(textSourceNode) || isPrivateIdentifier(textSourceNode) || isNumericLiteral(textSourceNode) || isJsxNamespacedName(textSourceNode)) {
    5172            8 :                 const text = isNumericLiteral(textSourceNode) ? textSourceNode.text : getTextOfNode(textSourceNode);
    5173            8 :                 return jsxAttributeEscape ? `"${escapeJsxAttributeString(text)}"` :
    5174            8 :                     neverAsciiEscape || (getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.NoAsciiEscaping) ? `"${escapeString(text)}"` :
    5175            8 :                     `"${escapeNonAsciiString(text)}"`;
    5176            8 :             }
    5177            8 :             else {
    5178            8 :                 return getLiteralTextOfNode(textSourceNode, neverAsciiEscape, jsxAttributeEscape);
    5179            8 :             }
    5180            8 :         }
    5181            8 : 
    5182            8 :         const flags = (neverAsciiEscape ? GetLiteralTextFlags.NeverAsciiEscape : 0)
    5183            8 :             | (jsxAttributeEscape ? GetLiteralTextFlags.JsxAttributeEscape : 0)
    5184            8 :             | (printerOptions.terminateUnterminatedLiterals ? GetLiteralTextFlags.TerminateUnterminatedLiterals : 0)
    5185            8 :             | (printerOptions.target && printerOptions.target >= ScriptTarget.ES2021 ? GetLiteralTextFlags.AllowNumericSeparator : 0);
    5186            8 : 
    5187            8 :         return getLiteralText(node, currentSourceFile, flags);
    5188            8 :     }
    5189            8 : 
    5190            8 :     /**
    5191            8 :      * Push a new name generation scope.
    5192            8 :      */
    5193            8 :     function pushNameGenerationScope(node: Node | undefined) {
    5194            8 :         privateNameTempFlagsStack.push(privateNameTempFlags);
    5195            8 :         privateNameTempFlags = TempFlags.Auto;
    5196            8 :         reservedPrivateNamesStack.push(reservedPrivateNames);
    5197            8 : 
    5198            8 :         if (node && getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.ReuseTempVariableScope) {
    5199            8 :             return;
    5200            8 :         }
    5201            8 : 
    5202            8 :         tempFlagsStack.push(tempFlags);
    5203            8 :         tempFlags = TempFlags.Auto;
    5204            8 :         formattedNameTempFlagsStack.push(formattedNameTempFlags);
    5205            8 :         formattedNameTempFlags = undefined;
    5206            8 :         reservedNamesStack.push(reservedNames);
    5207            8 :     }
    5208            8 : 
    5209            8 :     /**
    5210            8 :      * Pop the current name generation scope.
    5211            8 :      */
    5212            8 :     function popNameGenerationScope(node: Node | undefined) {
    5213            8 :         privateNameTempFlags = privateNameTempFlagsStack.pop()!;
    5214            8 :         reservedPrivateNames = reservedPrivateNamesStack.pop();
    5215            8 : 
    5216            8 :         if (node && getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.ReuseTempVariableScope) {
    5217            8 :             return;
    5218            8 :         }
    5219            8 : 
    5220            8 :         tempFlags = tempFlagsStack.pop()!;
    5221            8 :         formattedNameTempFlags = formattedNameTempFlagsStack.pop();
    5222            8 :         reservedNames = reservedNamesStack.pop();
    5223            8 :     }
    5224            8 : 
    5225            8 :     function reserveNameInNestedScopes(name: string) {
    5226            8 :         if (!reservedNames || reservedNames === lastOrUndefined(reservedNamesStack)) {
    5227            8 :             reservedNames = new Set();
    5228            8 :         }
    5229            8 :         reservedNames.add(name);
    5230            8 :     }
    5231            8 : 
    5232            8 :     function reservePrivateNameInNestedScopes(name: string) {
    5233            8 :         if (!reservedPrivateNames || reservedPrivateNames === lastOrUndefined(reservedPrivateNamesStack)) {
    5234            8 :             reservedPrivateNames = new Set();
    5235            8 :         }
    5236            8 :         reservedPrivateNames.add(name);
    5237            8 :     }
    5238            8 : 
    5239            8 :     function generateNames(node: Node | undefined) {
    5240            8 :         if (!node) return;
    5241            8 :         switch (node.kind) {
    5242            8 :             case SyntaxKind.Block:
    5243            8 :                 forEach((node as Block).statements, generateNames);
    5244            8 :                 break;
    5245            8 :             case SyntaxKind.LabeledStatement:
    5246            8 :             case SyntaxKind.WithStatement:
    5247            8 :             case SyntaxKind.DoStatement:
    5248            8 :             case SyntaxKind.WhileStatement:
    5249            8 :                 generateNames((node as LabeledStatement | WithStatement | DoStatement | WhileStatement).statement);
    5250            8 :                 break;
    5251            8 :             case SyntaxKind.IfStatement:
    5252            8 :                 generateNames((node as IfStatement).thenStatement);
    5253            8 :                 generateNames((node as IfStatement).elseStatement);
    5254            8 :                 break;
    5255            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ForStatement:
    5256            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ForOfStatement:
    5257            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ForInStatement:
    5258            8 :                 generateNames((node as ForStatement | ForInOrOfStatement).initializer);
    5259            8 :                 generateNames((node as ForStatement | ForInOrOfStatement).statement);
    5260            8 :                 break;
    5261            8 :             case SyntaxKind.SwitchStatement:
    5262            8 :                 generateNames((node as SwitchStatement).caseBlock);
    5263            8 :                 break;
    5264            8 :             case SyntaxKind.CaseBlock:
    5265            8 :                 forEach((node as CaseBlock).clauses, generateNames);
    5266            8 :                 break;
    5267            8 :             case SyntaxKind.CaseClause:
    5268            8 :             case SyntaxKind.DefaultClause:
    5269            8 :                 forEach((node as CaseOrDefaultClause).statements, generateNames);
    5270            8 :                 break;
    5271            8 :             case SyntaxKind.TryStatement:
    5272            8 :                 generateNames((node as TryStatement).tryBlock);
    5273            8 :                 generateNames((node as TryStatement).catchClause);
    5274            8 :                 generateNames((node as TryStatement).finallyBlock);
    5275            8 :                 break;
    5276            8 :             case SyntaxKind.CatchClause:
    5277            8 :                 generateNames((node as CatchClause).variableDeclaration);
    5278            8 :                 generateNames((node as CatchClause).block);
    5279            8 :                 break;
    5280            8 :             case SyntaxKind.VariableStatement:
    5281            8 :                 generateNames((node as VariableStatement).declarationList);
    5282            8 :                 break;
    5283            8 :             case SyntaxKind.VariableDeclarationList:
    5284            8 :                 forEach((node as VariableDeclarationList).declarations, generateNames);
    5285            8 :                 break;
    5286            8 :             case SyntaxKind.VariableDeclaration:
    5287            8 :             case SyntaxKind.Parameter:
    5288            8 :             case SyntaxKind.BindingElement:
    5289            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ClassDeclaration:
    5290            8 :                 generateNameIfNeeded((node as NamedDeclaration).name);
    5291            8 :                 break;
    5292            8 :             case SyntaxKind.FunctionDeclaration:
    5293            8 :                 generateNameIfNeeded((node as FunctionDeclaration).name);
    5294            8 :                 if (getEmitFlags(node) & EmitFlags.ReuseTempVariableScope) {
    5295            8 :                     forEach((node as FunctionDeclaration).parameters, generateNames);
    5296            8 :                     generateNames((node as FunctionDeclaration).body);
    5297            8 :                 }
    5298            8 :                 break;
    5299            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ObjectBindingPattern:
    5300            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ArrayBindingPattern:
    5301            8 :                 forEach((node as BindingPattern).elements, generateNames);
    5302            8 :                 break;
    5303            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ImportDeclaration:
    5304            8 :                 generateNames((node as ImportDeclaration).importClause);
    5305            8 :                 break;
    5306            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ImportClause:
    5307            8 :                 generateNameIfNeeded((node as ImportClause).name);
    5308            8 :                 generateNames((node as ImportClause).namedBindings);
    5309            8 :                 break;
    5310            8 :             case SyntaxKind.NamespaceImport:
    5311            8 :                 generateNameIfNeeded((node as NamespaceImport).name);
    5312            8 :                 break;
    5313            8 :             case SyntaxKind.NamespaceExport:
    5314            8 :                 generateNameIfNeeded((node as NamespaceExport).name);
    5315            8 :                 break;
    5316            8 :             case SyntaxKind.NamedImports:
    5317            8 :                 forEach((node as NamedImports).elements, generateNames);
    5318            8 :                 break;
    5319            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ImportSpecifier:
    5320            8 :                 generateNameIfNeeded((node as ImportSpecifier).propertyName || (node as ImportSpecifier).name);
    5321            8 :                 break;
    5322            8 :         }
    5323            8 :     }
    5324            8 : 
    5325            8 :     function generateMemberNames(node: Node | undefined) {
    5326            8 :         if (!node) return;
    5327            8 :         switch (node.kind) {
    5328            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PropertyAssignment:
    5329            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ShorthandPropertyAssignment:
    5330            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PropertyDeclaration:
    5331            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PropertySignature:
    5332            8 :             case SyntaxKind.MethodDeclaration:
    5333            8 :             case SyntaxKind.MethodSignature:
    5334            8 :             case SyntaxKind.GetAccessor:
    5335            8 :             case SyntaxKind.SetAccessor:
    5336            8 :                 generateNameIfNeeded((node as NamedDeclaration).name);
    5337            8 :                 break;
    5338            8 :         }
    5339            8 :     }
    5340            8 : 
    5341            8 :     function generateNameIfNeeded(name: DeclarationName | undefined) {
    5342            8 :         if (name) {
    5343            8 :             if (isGeneratedIdentifier(name) || isGeneratedPrivateIdentifier(name)) {
    5344            8 :                 generateName(name);
    5345            8 :             }
    5346            8 :             else if (isBindingPattern(name)) {
    5347            8 :                 generateNames(name);
    5348            8 :             }
    5349            8 :         }
    5350            8 :     }
    5351            8 : 
    5352            8 :     /**
    5353            8 :      * Generate the text for a generated identifier.
    5354            8 :      */
    5355            8 :     function generateName(name: GeneratedIdentifier | GeneratedPrivateIdentifier) {
    5356            8 :         const autoGenerate = name.emitNode.autoGenerate;
    5357            8 :         if ((autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.KindMask) === GeneratedIdentifierFlags.Node) {
    5358            8 :             // Node names generate unique names based on their original node
    5359            8 :             // and are cached based on that node's id.
    5360            8 :             return generateNameCached(getNodeForGeneratedName(name), isPrivateIdentifier(name), autoGenerate.flags, autoGenerate.prefix, autoGenerate.suffix);
    5361            8 :         }
    5362            8 :         else {
    5363            8 :             // Auto, Loop, and Unique names are cached based on their unique
    5364            8 :             // autoGenerateId.
    5365            8 :             const autoGenerateId = autoGenerate.id;
    5366            8 :             return autoGeneratedIdToGeneratedName[autoGenerateId] || (autoGeneratedIdToGeneratedName[autoGenerateId] = makeName(name));
    5367            8 :         }
    5368            8 :     }
    5369            8 : 
    5370            8 :     function generateNameCached(node: Node, privateName: boolean, flags?: GeneratedIdentifierFlags, prefix?: string | GeneratedNamePart, suffix?: string) {
    5371            8 :         const nodeId = getNodeId(node);
    5372            8 :         const cache = privateName ? nodeIdToGeneratedPrivateName : nodeIdToGeneratedName;
    5373            8 :         return cache[nodeId] || (cache[nodeId] = generateNameForNode(node, privateName, flags ?? GeneratedIdentifierFlags.None, formatGeneratedNamePart(prefix, generateName), formatGeneratedNamePart(suffix)));
    5374            8 :     }
    5375            8 : 
    5376            8 :     /**
    5377            8 :      * Returns a value indicating whether a name is unique globally, within the current file,
    5378            8 :      * or within the NameGenerator.
    5379            8 :      */
    5380            8 :     function isUniqueName(name: string, privateName: boolean): boolean {
    5381            8 :         return isFileLevelUniqueNameInCurrentFile(name, privateName)
    5382            8 :             && !isReservedName(name, privateName)
    5383            8 :             && !generatedNames.has(name);
    5384            8 :     }
    5385            8 : 
    5386            8 :     function isReservedName(name: string, privateName: boolean): boolean {
    5387            8 :         let set: Set<string> | undefined;
    5388            8 :         let stack: (Set<string> | undefined)[];
    5389            8 :         if (privateName) {
    5390            8 :             set = reservedPrivateNames;
    5391            8 :             stack = reservedPrivateNamesStack;
    5392            8 :         }
    5393            8 :         else {
    5394            8 :             set = reservedNames;
    5395            8 :             stack = reservedNamesStack;
    5396            8 :         }
    5397            8 : 
    5398            8 :         if (set?.has(name)) {
    5399            8 :             return true;
    5400            8 :         }
    5401            8 :         for (let i = stack.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    5402            8 :             if (set === stack[i]) {
    5403            8 :                 continue;
    5404            8 :             }
    5405            8 :             set = stack[i];
    5406            8 :             if (set?.has(name)) {
    5407            8 :                 return true;
    5408            8 :             }
    5409            8 :         }
    5410            8 :         return false;
    5411            8 :     }
    5412            8 : 
    5413            8 :     /**
    5414            8 :      * Returns a value indicating whether a name is unique globally or within the current file.
    5415            8 :      *
    5416            8 :      * @param _isPrivate (unused) this parameter exists to avoid an unnecessary adaptor frame in v8
    5417            8 :      * when `isfileLevelUniqueName` is passed as a callback to `makeUniqueName`.
    5418            8 :      */
    5419            8 :     function isFileLevelUniqueNameInCurrentFile(name: string, _isPrivate: boolean) {
    5420            8 :         return currentSourceFile ? isFileLevelUniqueName(currentSourceFile, name, hasGlobalName) : true;
    5421            8 :     }
    5422            8 : 
    5423            8 :     /**
    5424            8 :      * Returns a value indicating whether a name is unique within a container.
    5425            8 :      */
    5426            8 :     function isUniqueLocalName(name: string, container: HasLocals | undefined): boolean {
    5427            8 :         for (let node = container; node && isNodeDescendantOf(node, container); node = node.nextContainer) {
    5428            8 :             if (canHaveLocals(node) && node.locals) {
    5429            8 :                 const local = node.locals.get(escapeLeadingUnderscores(name));
    5430            8 :                 // We conservatively include alias symbols to cover cases where they're emitted as locals
    5431            8 :                 if (local && local.flags & (SymbolFlags.Value | SymbolFlags.ExportValue | SymbolFlags.Alias)) {
    5432            8 :                     return false;
    5433            8 :                 }
    5434            8 :             }
    5435            8 :         }
    5436            8 :         return true;
    5437            8 :     }
    5438            8 : 
    5439            8 :     function getTempFlags(formattedNameKey: string) {
    5440            8 :         switch (formattedNameKey) {
    5441            8 :             case "":
    5442            8 :                 return tempFlags;
    5443            8 :             case "#":
    5444            8 :                 return privateNameTempFlags;
    5445            8 :             default:
    5446            8 :                 return formattedNameTempFlags?.get(formattedNameKey) ?? TempFlags.Auto;
    5447            8 :         }
    5448            8 :     }
    5449            8 : 
    5450            8 :     function setTempFlags(formattedNameKey: string, flags: TempFlags) {
    5451            8 :         switch (formattedNameKey) {
    5452            8 :             case "":
    5453            8 :                 tempFlags = flags;
    5454            8 :                 break;
    5455            8 :             case "#":
    5456            8 :                 privateNameTempFlags = flags;
    5457            8 :                 break;
    5458            8 :             default:
    5459            8 :                 formattedNameTempFlags ??= new Map();
    5460            8 :                 formattedNameTempFlags.set(formattedNameKey, flags);
    5461            8 :                 break;
    5462            8 :         }
    5463            8 :     }
    5464            8 : 
    5465            8 :     /**
    5466            8 :      * Return the next available name in the pattern _a ... _z, _0, _1, ...
    5467            8 :      * TempFlags._i or TempFlags._n may be used to express a preference for that dedicated name.
    5468            8 :      * Note that names generated by makeTempVariableName and makeUniqueName will never conflict.
    5469            8 :      */
    5470            8 :     function makeTempVariableName(flags: TempFlags, reservedInNestedScopes: boolean, privateName: boolean, prefix: string, suffix: string): string {
    5471            8 :         if (prefix.length > 0 && prefix.charCodeAt(0) === CharacterCodes.hash) {
    5472            8 :             prefix = prefix.slice(1);
    5473            8 :         }
    5474            8 : 
    5475            8 :         // Generate a key to use to acquire a TempFlags counter based on the fixed portions of the generated name.
    5476            8 :         const key = formatGeneratedName(privateName, prefix, "", suffix);
    5477            8 :         let tempFlags = getTempFlags(key);
    5478            8 : 
    5479            8 :         if (flags && !(tempFlags & flags)) {
    5480            8 :             const name = flags === TempFlags._i ? "_i" : "_n";
    5481            8 :             const fullName = formatGeneratedName(privateName, prefix, name, suffix);
    5482            8 :             if (isUniqueName(fullName, privateName)) {
    5483            8 :                 tempFlags |= flags;
    5484            8 :                 if (privateName) {
    5485            8 :                     reservePrivateNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5486            8 :                 }
    5487            8 :                 else if (reservedInNestedScopes) {
    5488            8 :                     reserveNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5489            8 :                 }
    5490            8 :                 setTempFlags(key, tempFlags);
    5491            8 :                 return fullName;
    5492            8 :             }
    5493            8 :         }
    5494            8 : 
    5495            8 :         while (true) {
    5496            8 :             const count = tempFlags & TempFlags.CountMask;
    5497            8 :             tempFlags++;
    5498            8 :             // Skip over 'i' and 'n'
    5499            8 :             if (count !== 8 && count !== 13) {
    5500            8 :                 const name = count < 26
    5501            8 :                     ? "_" + String.fromCharCode(CharacterCodes.a + count)
    5502            8 :                     : "_" + (count - 26);
    5503            8 :                 const fullName = formatGeneratedName(privateName, prefix, name, suffix);
    5504            8 :                 if (isUniqueName(fullName, privateName)) {
    5505            8 :                     if (privateName) {
    5506            8 :                         reservePrivateNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5507            8 :                     }
    5508            8 :                     else if (reservedInNestedScopes) {
    5509            8 :                         reserveNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5510            8 :                     }
    5511            8 :                     setTempFlags(key, tempFlags);
    5512            8 :                     return fullName;
    5513            8 :                 }
    5514            8 :             }
    5515            8 :         }
    5516            8 :     }
    5517            8 : 
    5518            8 :     /**
    5519            8 :      * Generate a name that is unique within the current file and doesn't conflict with any names
    5520            8 :      * in global scope. The name is formed by adding an '_n' suffix to the specified base name,
    5521            8 :      * where n is a positive integer. Note that names generated by makeTempVariableName and
    5522            8 :      * makeUniqueName are guaranteed to never conflict.
    5523            8 :      * If `optimistic` is set, the first instance will use 'baseName' verbatim instead of 'baseName_1'
    5524            8 :      */
    5525            8 :     function makeUniqueName(baseName: string, checkFn: (name: string, privateName: boolean) => boolean = isUniqueName, optimistic: boolean, scoped: boolean, privateName: boolean, prefix: string, suffix: string): string {
    5526            8 :         if (baseName.length > 0 && baseName.charCodeAt(0) === CharacterCodes.hash) {
    5527            8 :             baseName = baseName.slice(1);
    5528            8 :         }
    5529            8 :         if (prefix.length > 0 && prefix.charCodeAt(0) === CharacterCodes.hash) {
    5530            8 :             prefix = prefix.slice(1);
    5531            8 :         }
    5532            8 :         if (optimistic) {
    5533            8 :             const fullName = formatGeneratedName(privateName, prefix, baseName, suffix);
    5534            8 :             if (checkFn(fullName, privateName)) {
    5535            8 :                 if (privateName) {
    5536            8 :                     reservePrivateNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5537            8 :                 }
    5538            8 :                 else if (scoped) {
    5539            8 :                     reserveNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5540            8 :                 }
    5541            8 :                 else {
    5542            8 :                     generatedNames.add(fullName);
    5543            8 :                 }
    5544            8 :                 return fullName;
    5545            8 :             }
    5546            8 :         }
    5547            8 :         // Find the first unique 'name_n', where n is a positive number
    5548            8 :         if (baseName.charCodeAt(baseName.length - 1) !== CharacterCodes._) {
    5549            8 :             baseName += "_";
    5550            8 :         }
    5551            8 :         let i = 1;
    5552            8 :         while (true) {
    5553            8 :             const fullName = formatGeneratedName(privateName, prefix, baseName + i, suffix);
    5554            8 :             if (checkFn(fullName, privateName)) {
    5555            8 :                 if (privateName) {
    5556            8 :                     reservePrivateNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5557            8 :                 }
    5558            8 :                 else if (scoped) {
    5559            8 :                     reserveNameInNestedScopes(fullName);
    5560            8 :                 }
    5561            8 :                 else {
    5562            8 :                     generatedNames.add(fullName);
    5563            8 :                 }
    5564            8 :                 return fullName;
    5565            8 :             }
    5566            8 :             i++;
    5567            8 :         }
    5568            8 :     }
    5569            8 : 
    5570            8 :     function makeFileLevelOptimisticUniqueName(name: string) {
    5571            8 :         return makeUniqueName(name, isFileLevelUniqueNameInCurrentFile, /*optimistic*/ true, /*scoped*/ false, /*privateName*/ false, /*prefix*/ "", /*suffix*/ "");
    5572            8 :     }
    5573            8 : 
    5574            8 :     /**
    5575            8 :      * Generates a unique name for a ModuleDeclaration or EnumDeclaration.
    5576            8 :      */
    5577            8 :     function generateNameForModuleOrEnum(node: ModuleDeclaration | EnumDeclaration) {
    5578            8 :         const name = getTextOfNode(node.name);
    5579            8 :         // Use module/enum name itself if it is unique, otherwise make a unique variation
    5580            8 :         return isUniqueLocalName(name, tryCast(node, canHaveLocals)) ? name : makeUniqueName(name, isUniqueName, /*optimistic*/ false, /*scoped*/ false, /*privateName*/ false, /*prefix*/ "", /*suffix*/ "");
    5581            8 :     }
    5582            8 : 
    5583            8 :     /**
    5584            8 :      * Generates a unique name for an ImportDeclaration or ExportDeclaration.
    5585            8 :      */
    5586            8 :     function generateNameForImportOrExportDeclaration(node: ImportDeclaration | ExportDeclaration) {
    5587            8 :         const expr = getExternalModuleName(node)!; // TODO: GH#18217
    5588            8 :         const baseName = isStringLiteral(expr) ?
    5589            8 :             makeIdentifierFromModuleName(expr.text) : "module";
    5590            8 :         return makeUniqueName(baseName, isUniqueName, /*optimistic*/ false, /*scoped*/ false, /*privateName*/ false, /*prefix*/ "", /*suffix*/ "");
    5591            8 :     }
    5592            8 : 
    5593            8 :     /**
    5594            8 :      * Generates a unique name for a default export.
    5595            8 :      */
    5596            8 :     function generateNameForExportDefault() {
    5597            8 :         return makeUniqueName("default", isUniqueName, /*optimistic*/ false, /*scoped*/ false, /*privateName*/ false, /*prefix*/ "", /*suffix*/ "");
    5598            8 :     }
    5599            8 : 
    5600            8 :     /**
    5601            8 :      * Generates a unique name for a class expression.
    5602            8 :      */
    5603            8 :     function generateNameForClassExpression() {
    5604            8 :         return makeUniqueName("class", isUniqueName, /*optimistic*/ false, /*scoped*/ false, /*privateName*/ false, /*prefix*/ "", /*suffix*/ "");
    5605            8 :     }
    5606            8 : 
    5607            8 :     function generateNameForMethodOrAccessor(node: MethodDeclaration | AccessorDeclaration, privateName: boolean, prefix: string, suffix: string) {
    5608            8 :         if (isIdentifier(node.name)) {
    5609            8 :             return generateNameCached(node.name, privateName);
    5610            8 :         }
    5611            8 :         return makeTempVariableName(TempFlags.Auto, /*reservedInNestedScopes*/ false, privateName, prefix, suffix);
    5612            8 :     }
    5613            8 : 
    5614            8 :     /**
    5615            8 :      * Generates a unique name from a node.
    5616            8 :      */
    5617            8 :     function generateNameForNode(node: Node, privateName: boolean, flags: GeneratedIdentifierFlags, prefix: string, suffix: string): string {
    5618            8 :         switch (node.kind) {
    5619            8 :             case SyntaxKind.Identifier:
    5620            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PrivateIdentifier:
    5621            8 :                 return makeUniqueName(
    5622            8 :                     getTextOfNode(node as Identifier),
    5623            8 :                     isUniqueName,
    5624            8 :                     !!(flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.Optimistic),
    5625            8 :                     !!(flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.ReservedInNestedScopes),
    5626            8 :                     privateName,
    5627            8 :                     prefix,
    5628            8 :                     suffix,
    5629            8 :                 );
    5630            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ModuleDeclaration:
    5631            8 :             case SyntaxKind.EnumDeclaration:
    5632            8 :                 Debug.assert(!prefix && !suffix && !privateName);
    5633            8 :                 return generateNameForModuleOrEnum(node as ModuleDeclaration | EnumDeclaration);
    5634            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ImportDeclaration:
    5635            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ExportDeclaration:
    5636            8 :                 Debug.assert(!prefix && !suffix && !privateName);
    5637            8 :                 return generateNameForImportOrExportDeclaration(node as ImportDeclaration | ExportDeclaration);
    5638            8 :             case SyntaxKind.FunctionDeclaration:
    5639            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ClassDeclaration: {
    5640            8 :                 Debug.assert(!prefix && !suffix && !privateName);
    5641            8 :                 const name = (node as ClassDeclaration | FunctionDeclaration).name;
    5642            8 :                 if (name && !isGeneratedIdentifier(name)) {
    5643            8 :                     return generateNameForNode(name, /*privateName*/ false, flags, prefix, suffix);
    5644            8 :                 }
    5645            8 :                 return generateNameForExportDefault();
    5646            8 :             }
    5647            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ExportAssignment:
    5648            8 :                 Debug.assert(!prefix && !suffix && !privateName);
    5649            8 :                 return generateNameForExportDefault();
    5650            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ClassExpression:
    5651            8 :                 Debug.assert(!prefix && !suffix && !privateName);
    5652            8 :                 return generateNameForClassExpression();
    5653            8 :             case SyntaxKind.MethodDeclaration:
    5654            8 :             case SyntaxKind.GetAccessor:
    5655            8 :             case SyntaxKind.SetAccessor:
    5656            8 :                 return generateNameForMethodOrAccessor(node as MethodDeclaration | AccessorDeclaration, privateName, prefix, suffix);
    5657            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ComputedPropertyName:
    5658            8 :                 return makeTempVariableName(TempFlags.Auto, /*reservedInNestedScopes*/ true, privateName, prefix, suffix);
    5659            8 :             default:
    5660            8 :                 return makeTempVariableName(TempFlags.Auto, /*reservedInNestedScopes*/ false, privateName, prefix, suffix);
    5661            8 :         }
    5662            8 :     }
    5663            8 : 
    5664            8 :     /**
    5665            8 :      * Generates a unique identifier for a node.
    5666            8 :      */
    5667            8 :     function makeName(name: GeneratedIdentifier | GeneratedPrivateIdentifier) {
    5668            8 :         const autoGenerate = name.emitNode.autoGenerate;
    5669            8 :         const prefix = formatGeneratedNamePart(autoGenerate.prefix, generateName);
    5670            8 :         const suffix = formatGeneratedNamePart(autoGenerate.suffix);
    5671            8 :         switch (autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.KindMask) {
    5672            8 :             case GeneratedIdentifierFlags.Auto:
    5673            8 :                 return makeTempVariableName(TempFlags.Auto, !!(autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.ReservedInNestedScopes), isPrivateIdentifier(name), prefix, suffix);
    5674            8 :             case GeneratedIdentifierFlags.Loop:
    5675            8 :                 Debug.assertNode(name, isIdentifier);
    5676            8 :                 return makeTempVariableName(TempFlags._i, !!(autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.ReservedInNestedScopes), /*privateName*/ false, prefix, suffix);
    5677            8 :             case GeneratedIdentifierFlags.Unique:
    5678            8 :                 return makeUniqueName(
    5679            8 :                     idText(name),
    5680            8 :                     (autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.FileLevel) ? isFileLevelUniqueNameInCurrentFile : isUniqueName,
    5681            8 :                     !!(autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.Optimistic),
    5682            8 :                     !!(autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.ReservedInNestedScopes),
    5683            8 :                     isPrivateIdentifier(name),
    5684            8 :                     prefix,
    5685            8 :                     suffix,
    5686            8 :                 );
    5687            8 :         }
    5688            8 : 
    5689            8 :         return Debug.fail(`Unsupported GeneratedIdentifierKind: ${Debug.formatEnum(autoGenerate.flags & GeneratedIdentifierFlags.KindMask, (ts as any).GeneratedIdentifierFlags, /*isFlags*/ true)}.`);
    5690            8 :     }
    5691            8 : 
    5692            8 :     // Comments
    5693            8 : 
    5694            8 :     function pipelineEmitWithComments(hint: EmitHint, node: Node) {
    5695            8 :         const pipelinePhase = getNextPipelinePhase(PipelinePhase.Comments, hint, node);
    5696            8 :         const savedContainerPos = containerPos;
    5697            8 :         const savedContainerEnd = containerEnd;
    5698            8 :         const savedDeclarationListContainerEnd = declarationListContainerEnd;
    5699            8 :         emitCommentsBeforeNode(node);
    5700            8 :         pipelinePhase(hint, node);
    5701            8 :         emitCommentsAfterNode(node, savedContainerPos, savedContainerEnd, savedDeclarationListContainerEnd);
    5702            8 :     }
    5703            8 : 
    5704            8 :     function emitCommentsBeforeNode(node: Node) {
    5705            8 :         const emitFlags = getEmitFlags(node);
    5706            8 :         const commentRange = getCommentRange(node);
    5707            8 : 
    5708            8 :         // Emit leading comments
    5709            8 :         emitLeadingCommentsOfNode(node, emitFlags, commentRange.pos, commentRange.end);
    5710            8 :         if (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoNestedComments) {
    5711            8 :             commentsDisabled = true;
    5712            8 :         }
    5713            8 :     }
    5714            8 : 
    5715            8 :     function emitCommentsAfterNode(node: Node, savedContainerPos: number, savedContainerEnd: number, savedDeclarationListContainerEnd: number) {
    5716            8 :         const emitFlags = getEmitFlags(node);
    5717            8 :         const commentRange = getCommentRange(node);
    5718            8 : 
    5719            8 :         // Emit trailing comments
    5720            8 :         if (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoNestedComments) {
    5721            8 :             commentsDisabled = false;
    5722            8 :         }
    5723            8 :         emitTrailingCommentsOfNode(node, emitFlags, commentRange.pos, commentRange.end, savedContainerPos, savedContainerEnd, savedDeclarationListContainerEnd);
    5724            8 :         const typeNode = getTypeNode(node);
    5725            8 :         if (typeNode) {
    5726            8 :             emitTrailingCommentsOfNode(node, emitFlags, typeNode.pos, typeNode.end, savedContainerPos, savedContainerEnd, savedDeclarationListContainerEnd);
    5727            8 :         }
    5728            8 :     }
    5729            8 : 
    5730            8 :     function emitLeadingCommentsOfNode(node: Node, emitFlags: EmitFlags, pos: number, end: number) {
    5731            8 :         enterComment();
    5732            8 :         hasWrittenComment = false;
    5733            8 : 
    5734            8 :         // We have to explicitly check that the node is JsxText because if the compilerOptions.jsx is "preserve" we will not do any transformation.
    5735            8 :         // It is expensive to walk entire tree just to set one kind of node to have no comments.
    5736            8 :         const skipLeadingComments = pos < 0 || (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoLeadingComments) !== 0 || node.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxText;
    5737            8 :         const skipTrailingComments = end < 0 || (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingComments) !== 0 || node.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxText;
    5738            8 : 
    5739            8 :         // Save current container state on the stack.
    5740            8 :         if ((pos > 0 || end > 0) && pos !== end) {
    5741            8 :             // Emit leading comments if the position is not synthesized and the node
    5742            8 :             // has not opted out from emitting leading comments.
    5743            8 :             if (!skipLeadingComments) {
    5744            8 :                 emitLeadingComments(pos, /*isEmittedNode*/ node.kind !== SyntaxKind.NotEmittedStatement);
    5745            8 :             }
    5746            8 : 
    5747            8 :             if (!skipLeadingComments || (pos >= 0 && (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoLeadingComments) !== 0)) {
    5748            8 :                 // Advance the container position if comments get emitted or if they've been disabled explicitly using NoLeadingComments.
    5749            8 :                 containerPos = pos;
    5750            8 :             }
    5751            8 : 
    5752            8 :             if (!skipTrailingComments || (end >= 0 && (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingComments) !== 0)) {
    5753            8 :                 // As above.
    5754            8 :                 containerEnd = end;
    5755            8 : 
    5756            8 :                 // To avoid invalid comment emit in a down-level binding pattern, we
    5757            8 :                 // keep track of the last declaration list container's end
    5758            8 :                 if (node.kind === SyntaxKind.VariableDeclarationList) {
    5759            8 :                     declarationListContainerEnd = end;
    5760            8 :                 }
    5761            8 :             }
    5762            8 :         }
    5763            8 :         forEach(getSyntheticLeadingComments(node), emitLeadingSynthesizedComment);
    5764            8 :         exitComment();
    5765            8 :     }
    5766            8 : 
    5767            8 :     function emitTrailingCommentsOfNode(node: Node, emitFlags: EmitFlags, pos: number, end: number, savedContainerPos: number, savedContainerEnd: number, savedDeclarationListContainerEnd: number) {
    5768            8 :         enterComment();
    5769            8 :         const skipTrailingComments = end < 0 || (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingComments) !== 0 || node.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxText;
    5770            8 :         forEach(getSyntheticTrailingComments(node), emitTrailingSynthesizedComment);
    5771            8 :         if ((pos > 0 || end > 0) && pos !== end) {
    5772            8 :             // Restore previous container state.
    5773            8 :             containerPos = savedContainerPos;
    5774            8 :             containerEnd = savedContainerEnd;
    5775            8 :             declarationListContainerEnd = savedDeclarationListContainerEnd;
    5776            8 : 
    5777            8 :             // Emit trailing comments if the position is not synthesized and the node
    5778            8 :             // has not opted out from emitting leading comments and is an emitted node.
    5779            8 :             if (!skipTrailingComments && node.kind !== SyntaxKind.NotEmittedStatement) {
    5780            8 :                 emitTrailingComments(end);
    5781            8 :             }
    5782            8 :         }
    5783            8 :         exitComment();
    5784            8 :     }
    5785            8 : 
    5786            8 :     function emitLeadingSynthesizedComment(comment: SynthesizedComment) {
    5787            8 :         if (comment.hasLeadingNewline || comment.kind === SyntaxKind.SingleLineCommentTrivia) {
    5788            8 :             writer.writeLine();
    5789            8 :         }
    5790            8 :         writeSynthesizedComment(comment);
    5791            8 :         if (comment.hasTrailingNewLine || comment.kind === SyntaxKind.SingleLineCommentTrivia) {
    5792            8 :             writer.writeLine();
    5793            8 :         }
    5794            8 :         else {
    5795            8 :             writer.writeSpace(" ");
    5796            8 :         }
    5797            8 :     }
    5798            8 : 
    5799            8 :     function emitTrailingSynthesizedComment(comment: SynthesizedComment) {
    5800            8 :         if (!writer.isAtStartOfLine()) {
    5801            8 :             writer.writeSpace(" ");
    5802            8 :         }
    5803            8 :         writeSynthesizedComment(comment);
    5804            8 :         if (comment.hasTrailingNewLine) {
    5805            8 :             writer.writeLine();
    5806            8 :         }
    5807            8 :     }
    5808            8 : 
    5809            8 :     function writeSynthesizedComment(comment: SynthesizedComment) {
    5810            8 :         const text = formatSynthesizedComment(comment);
    5811            8 :         const lineMap = comment.kind === SyntaxKind.MultiLineCommentTrivia ? computeLineStarts(text) : undefined;
    5812            8 :         writeCommentRange(text, lineMap!, writer, 0, text.length, newLine);
    5813            8 :     }
    5814            8 : 
    5815            8 :     function formatSynthesizedComment(comment: SynthesizedComment) {
    5816            8 :         return comment.kind === SyntaxKind.MultiLineCommentTrivia
    5817            8 :             ? `/*${comment.text}*/`
    5818            8 :             : `//${comment.text}`;
    5819            8 :     }
    5820            8 : 
    5821            8 :     function emitBodyWithDetachedComments<T extends Node>(node: T, detachedRange: TextRange, emitCallback: (node: T) => void) {
    5822            8 :         enterComment();
    5823            8 :         const { pos, end } = detachedRange;
    5824            8 :         const emitFlags = getEmitFlags(node);
    5825            8 :         const skipLeadingComments = pos < 0 || (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoLeadingComments) !== 0;
    5826            8 :         const skipTrailingComments = commentsDisabled || end < 0 || (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingComments) !== 0;
    5827            8 :         if (!skipLeadingComments) {
    5828            8 :             emitDetachedCommentsAndUpdateCommentsInfo(detachedRange);
    5829            8 :         }
    5830            8 : 
    5831            8 :         exitComment();
    5832            8 :         if (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoNestedComments && !commentsDisabled) {
    5833            8 :             commentsDisabled = true;
    5834            8 :             emitCallback(node);
    5835            8 :             commentsDisabled = false;
    5836            8 :         }
    5837            8 :         else {
    5838            8 :             emitCallback(node);
    5839            8 :         }
    5840            8 : 
    5841            8 :         enterComment();
    5842            8 :         if (!skipTrailingComments) {
    5843            8 :             emitLeadingComments(detachedRange.end, /*isEmittedNode*/ true);
    5844            8 :             if (hasWrittenComment && !writer.isAtStartOfLine()) {
    5845            8 :                 writer.writeLine();
    5846            8 :             }
    5847            8 :         }
    5848            8 :         exitComment();
    5849            8 :     }
    5850            8 : 
    5851            8 :     function originalNodesHaveSameParent(nodeA: Node, nodeB: Node) {
    5852            8 :         nodeA = getOriginalNode(nodeA);
    5853            8 :         // For performance, do not call `getOriginalNode` for `nodeB` if `nodeA` doesn't even
    5854            8 :         // have a parent node.
    5855            8 :         return nodeA.parent && nodeA.parent === getOriginalNode(nodeB).parent;
    5856            8 :     }
    5857            8 : 
    5858            8 :     function siblingNodePositionsAreComparable(previousNode: Node, nextNode: Node) {
    5859            8 :         if (nextNode.pos < previousNode.end) {
    5860            8 :             return false;
    5861            8 :         }
    5862            8 : 
    5863            8 :         previousNode = getOriginalNode(previousNode);
    5864            8 :         nextNode = getOriginalNode(nextNode);
    5865            8 :         const parent = previousNode.parent;
    5866            8 :         if (!parent || parent !== nextNode.parent) {
    5867            8 :             return false;
    5868            8 :         }
    5869            8 : 
    5870            8 :         const parentNodeArray = getContainingNodeArray(previousNode);
    5871            8 :         const prevNodeIndex = parentNodeArray?.indexOf(previousNode);
    5872            8 :         return prevNodeIndex !== undefined && prevNodeIndex > -1 && parentNodeArray!.indexOf(nextNode) === prevNodeIndex + 1;
    5873            8 :     }
    5874            8 : 
    5875            8 :     function emitLeadingComments(pos: number, isEmittedNode: boolean) {
    5876            8 :         hasWrittenComment = false;
    5877            8 : 
    5878            8 :         if (isEmittedNode) {
    5879            8 :             if (pos === 0 && currentSourceFile?.isDeclarationFile) {
    5880            8 :                 forEachLeadingCommentToEmit(pos, emitNonTripleSlashLeadingComment);
    5881            8 :             }
    5882            8 :             else {
    5883            8 :                 forEachLeadingCommentToEmit(pos, emitLeadingComment);
    5884            8 :             }
    5885            8 :         }
    5886            8 :         else if (pos === 0) {
    5887            8 :             // If the node will not be emitted in JS, remove all the comments(normal, pinned and ///) associated with the node,
    5888            8 :             // unless it is a triple slash comment at the top of the file.
    5889            8 :             // For Example:
    5890            8 :             //      /// <reference-path ...>
    5891            8 :             //      declare var x;
    5892            8 :             //      /// <reference-path ...>
    5893            8 :             //      interface F {}
    5894            8 :             //  The first /// will NOT be removed while the second one will be removed even though both node will not be emitted
    5895            8 :             forEachLeadingCommentToEmit(pos, emitTripleSlashLeadingComment);
    5896            8 :         }
    5897            8 :     }
    5898            8 : 
    5899            8 :     function emitTripleSlashLeadingComment(commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean, rangePos: number) {
    5900            8 :         if (isTripleSlashComment(commentPos, commentEnd)) {
    5901            8 :             emitLeadingComment(commentPos, commentEnd, kind, hasTrailingNewLine, rangePos);
    5902            8 :         }
    5903            8 :     }
    5904            8 : 
    5905            8 :     function emitNonTripleSlashLeadingComment(commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean, rangePos: number) {
    5906            8 :         if (!isTripleSlashComment(commentPos, commentEnd)) {
    5907            8 :             emitLeadingComment(commentPos, commentEnd, kind, hasTrailingNewLine, rangePos);
    5908            8 :         }
    5909            8 :     }
    5910            8 : 
    5911            8 :     function shouldWriteComment(text: string, pos: number) {
    5912            8 :         if (printerOptions.onlyPrintJsDocStyle) {
    5913            8 :             return (isJSDocLikeText(text, pos) || isPinnedComment(text, pos));
    5914            8 :         }
    5915            8 :         return true;
    5916            8 :     }
    5917            8 : 
    5918            8 :     function emitLeadingComment(commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean, rangePos: number) {
    5919            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile || !shouldWriteComment(currentSourceFile.text, commentPos)) return;
    5920            8 :         if (!hasWrittenComment) {
    5921            8 :             emitNewLineBeforeLeadingCommentOfPosition(getCurrentLineMap(), writer, rangePos, commentPos);
    5922            8 :             hasWrittenComment = true;
    5923            8 :         }
    5924            8 : 
    5925            8 :         // Leading comments are emitted at /*leading comment1 */space/*leading comment*/space
    5926            8 :         emitPos(commentPos);
    5927            8 :         writeCommentRange(currentSourceFile.text, getCurrentLineMap(), writer, commentPos, commentEnd, newLine);
    5928            8 :         emitPos(commentEnd);
    5929            8 : 
    5930            8 :         if (hasTrailingNewLine) {
    5931            8 :             writer.writeLine();
    5932            8 :         }
    5933            8 :         else if (kind === SyntaxKind.MultiLineCommentTrivia) {
    5934            8 :             writer.writeSpace(" ");
    5935            8 :         }
    5936            8 :     }
    5937            8 : 
    5938            8 :     function emitLeadingCommentsOfPosition(pos: number) {
    5939            8 :         if (commentsDisabled || pos === -1) {
    5940            8 :             return;
    5941            8 :         }
    5942            8 : 
    5943            8 :         emitLeadingComments(pos, /*isEmittedNode*/ true);
    5944            8 :     }
    5945            8 : 
    5946            8 :     function emitTrailingComments(pos: number) {
    5947            8 :         forEachTrailingCommentToEmit(pos, emitTrailingComment);
    5948            8 :     }
    5949            8 : 
    5950            8 :     function emitTrailingComment(commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, _kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean) {
    5951            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile || !shouldWriteComment(currentSourceFile.text, commentPos)) return;
    5952            8 :         // trailing comments are emitted at space/*trailing comment1 */space/*trailing comment2*/
    5953            8 :         if (!writer.isAtStartOfLine()) {
    5954            8 :             writer.writeSpace(" ");
    5955            8 :         }
    5956            8 : 
    5957            8 :         emitPos(commentPos);
    5958            8 :         writeCommentRange(currentSourceFile.text, getCurrentLineMap(), writer, commentPos, commentEnd, newLine);
    5959            8 :         emitPos(commentEnd);
    5960            8 : 
    5961            8 :         if (hasTrailingNewLine) {
    5962            8 :             writer.writeLine();
    5963            8 :         }
    5964            8 :     }
    5965            8 : 
    5966            8 :     function emitTrailingCommentsOfPosition(pos: number, prefixSpace?: boolean, forceNoNewline?: boolean) {
    5967            8 :         if (commentsDisabled) {
    5968            8 :             return;
    5969            8 :         }
    5970            8 :         enterComment();
    5971            8 :         forEachTrailingCommentToEmit(pos, prefixSpace ? emitTrailingComment : forceNoNewline ? emitTrailingCommentOfPositionNoNewline : emitTrailingCommentOfPosition);
    5972            8 :         exitComment();
    5973            8 :     }
    5974            8 : 
    5975            8 :     function emitTrailingCommentOfPositionNoNewline(commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, kind: SyntaxKind) {
    5976            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile) return;
    5977            8 :         // trailing comments of a position are emitted at /*trailing comment1 */space/*trailing comment*/space
    5978            8 : 
    5979            8 :         emitPos(commentPos);
    5980            8 :         writeCommentRange(currentSourceFile.text, getCurrentLineMap(), writer, commentPos, commentEnd, newLine);
    5981            8 :         emitPos(commentEnd);
    5982            8 : 
    5983            8 :         if (kind === SyntaxKind.SingleLineCommentTrivia) {
    5984            8 :             writer.writeLine(); // still write a newline for single-line comments, so closing tokens aren't written on the same line
    5985            8 :         }
    5986            8 :     }
    5987            8 : 
    5988            8 :     function emitTrailingCommentOfPosition(commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, _kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean) {
    5989            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile) return;
    5990            8 :         // trailing comments of a position are emitted at /*trailing comment1 */space/*trailing comment*/space
    5991            8 : 
    5992            8 :         emitPos(commentPos);
    5993            8 :         writeCommentRange(currentSourceFile.text, getCurrentLineMap(), writer, commentPos, commentEnd, newLine);
    5994            8 :         emitPos(commentEnd);
    5995            8 : 
    5996            8 :         if (hasTrailingNewLine) {
    5997            8 :             writer.writeLine();
    5998            8 :         }
    5999            8 :         else {
    6000            8 :             writer.writeSpace(" ");
    6001            8 :         }
    6002            8 :     }
    6003            8 : 
    6004            8 :     function forEachLeadingCommentToEmit(pos: number, cb: (commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean, rangePos: number) => void) {
    6005            8 :         // Emit the leading comments only if the container's pos doesn't match because the container should take care of emitting these comments
    6006            8 :         if (currentSourceFile && (containerPos === -1 || pos !== containerPos)) {
    6007            8 :             if (hasDetachedComments(pos)) {
    6008            8 :                 forEachLeadingCommentWithoutDetachedComments(cb);
    6009            8 :             }
    6010            8 :             else {
    6011            8 :                 forEachLeadingCommentRange(currentSourceFile.text, pos, cb, /*state*/ pos);
    6012            8 :             }
    6013            8 :         }
    6014            8 :     }
    6015            8 : 
    6016            8 :     function forEachTrailingCommentToEmit(end: number, cb: (commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean) => void) {
    6017            8 :         // Emit the trailing comments only if the container's end doesn't match because the container should take care of emitting these comments
    6018            8 :         if (currentSourceFile && (containerEnd === -1 || (end !== containerEnd && end !== declarationListContainerEnd))) {
    6019            8 :             forEachTrailingCommentRange(currentSourceFile.text, end, cb);
    6020            8 :         }
    6021            8 :     }
    6022            8 : 
    6023            8 :     function hasDetachedComments(pos: number) {
    6024            8 :         return detachedCommentsInfo !== undefined && last(detachedCommentsInfo).nodePos === pos;
    6025            8 :     }
    6026            8 : 
    6027            8 :     function forEachLeadingCommentWithoutDetachedComments(cb: (commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, kind: SyntaxKind, hasTrailingNewLine: boolean, rangePos: number) => void) {
    6028            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile) return;
    6029            8 :         // get the leading comments from detachedPos
    6030            8 :         const pos = last(detachedCommentsInfo!).detachedCommentEndPos;
    6031            8 :         if (detachedCommentsInfo!.length - 1) {
    6032            8 :             detachedCommentsInfo!.pop();
    6033            8 :         }
    6034            8 :         else {
    6035            8 :             detachedCommentsInfo = undefined;
    6036            8 :         }
    6037            8 : 
    6038            8 :         forEachLeadingCommentRange(currentSourceFile.text, pos, cb, /*state*/ pos);
    6039            8 :     }
    6040            8 : 
    6041            8 :     function emitDetachedCommentsAndUpdateCommentsInfo(range: TextRange) {
    6042            8 :         const currentDetachedCommentInfo = currentSourceFile && emitDetachedComments(currentSourceFile.text, getCurrentLineMap(), writer, emitComment, range, newLine, commentsDisabled);
    6043            8 :         if (currentDetachedCommentInfo) {
    6044            8 :             if (detachedCommentsInfo) {
    6045            8 :                 detachedCommentsInfo.push(currentDetachedCommentInfo);
    6046            8 :             }
    6047            8 :             else {
    6048            8 :                 detachedCommentsInfo = [currentDetachedCommentInfo];
    6049            8 :             }
    6050            8 :         }
    6051            8 :     }
    6052            8 : 
    6053            8 :     function emitComment(text: string, lineMap: readonly number[], writer: EmitTextWriter, commentPos: number, commentEnd: number, newLine: string) {
    6054            8 :         if (!currentSourceFile || !shouldWriteComment(currentSourceFile.text, commentPos)) return;
    6055            8 :         emitPos(commentPos);
    6056            8 :         writeCommentRange(text, lineMap, writer, commentPos, commentEnd, newLine);
    6057            8 :         emitPos(commentEnd);
    6058            8 :     }
    6059            8 : 
    6060            8 :     /**
    6061            8 :      * Determine if the given comment is a triple-slash
    6062            8 :      *
    6063            8 :      * @return true if the comment is a triple-slash comment else false
    6064            8 :      */
    6065            8 :     function isTripleSlashComment(commentPos: number, commentEnd: number) {
    6066            8 :         return !!currentSourceFile && isRecognizedTripleSlashComment(currentSourceFile.text, commentPos, commentEnd);
    6067            8 :     }

    6069            8 :     // Source Maps
    6070            8 :     function pipelineEmitWithSourceMaps(hint: EmitHint, node: Node) {
    6071            8 :         const pipelinePhase = getNextPipelinePhase(PipelinePhase.SourceMaps, hint, node);
    6072            8 :         emitSourceMapsBeforeNode(node);
    6073            8 :         pipelinePhase(hint, node);
    6074            8 :         emitSourceMapsAfterNode(node);
    6075            8 :     }
    6076            8 : 
    6077            8 :     function emitSourceMapsBeforeNode(node: Node) {
    6078            8 :         const emitFlags = getEmitFlags(node);
    6079            8 :         const sourceMapRange = getSourceMapRange(node);
    6080            8 : 
    6081            8 :         // Emit leading sourcemap
    6082            8 :         const source = sourceMapRange.source || sourceMapSource;
    6083            8 :         if (
    6084            8 :             node.kind !== SyntaxKind.NotEmittedStatement
    6085            8 :             && (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoLeadingSourceMap) === 0
    6086            8 :             && sourceMapRange.pos >= 0
    6087            8 :         ) {
    6088            8 :             emitSourcePos(sourceMapRange.source || sourceMapSource, skipSourceTrivia(source, sourceMapRange.pos));
    6089            8 :         }
    6090            8 :         if (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoNestedSourceMaps) {
    6091            8 :             sourceMapsDisabled = true;
    6092            8 :         }
    6093            8 :     }
    6094            8 : 
    6095            8 :     function emitSourceMapsAfterNode(node: Node) {
    6096            8 :         const emitFlags = getEmitFlags(node);
    6097            8 :         const sourceMapRange = getSourceMapRange(node);
    6098            8 : 
    6099            8 :         // Emit trailing sourcemap
    6100            8 :         if (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoNestedSourceMaps) {
    6101            8 :             sourceMapsDisabled = false;
    6102            8 :         }
    6103            8 :         if (
    6104            8 :             node.kind !== SyntaxKind.NotEmittedStatement
    6105            8 :             && (emitFlags & EmitFlags.NoTrailingSourceMap) === 0
    6106            8 :             && sourceMapRange.end >= 0
    6107            8 :         ) {
    6108            8 :             emitSourcePos(sourceMapRange.source || sourceMapSource, sourceMapRange.end);
    6109            8 :         }
    6110            8 :     }
    6111            8 : 
    6112            8 :     /**
